    जो विशेषण संज्ञा की संख्या या क्रम का बोध कराए, उसे Adjective of Number कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    one boy

    two girls

    first chapter

    second player

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Cardinal Number

    Quantity बताता है।

    Examples: one, two, three

  • ---

    • Ordinal Number

    Position बताता है।

    Examples: first, second, third

  • ---

    • Difference Between Quantity and Number

    Quantity

    अंदाज़ा

    some water

  • ---

    • Number

    Exact counting

    three books

  • ---

    • 4. Demonstrative Adjective

    (संकेतवाचक विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adjective that points out a noun is called a demonstrative adjective.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो विशेषण किसी noun की ओर संकेत करे, उसे Demonstrative Adjective कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    this book

    that boy

    these apples

    those houses

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Near

    this, these

  • ---

    • Far

    that, those

  • ---

    • Demonstrative Adjective vs Demonstrative Pronoun

    Demonstrative Adjective

    this book

    यहाँ: book noun मौजूद है।

  • ---

    • Demonstrative Pronoun

    This is my book.

    यहाँ: noun नहीं है।

  • ---

    • 5. Possessive Adjective

    (अधिकारवाचक विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adjective that shows possession or ownership is called a possessive adjective.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो विशेषण अधिकार या संबंध का बोध कराए, उसे Possessive Adjective कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    my book

    your pen

    his car

    their house

  • ---

    • 6. Interrogative Adjective

    (प्रश्नवाचक विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adjective used with a noun to ask questions is called an interrogative adjective.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो विशेषण noun के साथ प्रश्न पूछने के लिए प्रयोग किया जाए, उसे Interrogative Adjective कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    which book

    what subject

    whose bag

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Which book is yours?

    What language do you speak?

  • ---

    • Degree of Adjective

    (विशेषण की डिग्री)

    Adjective की तुलना तीन स्तरों पर की जाती है।

  • ---

    • 1. Positive Degree

    सामान्य अवस्था।

    Example:

    Ram is tall.

  • ---

    • 2. Comparative Degree

    दो लोगों/वस्तुओं की तुलना।

    Example:

    Ram is taller than Mohan.

  • ---

    • 3. Superlative Degree

    सबसे अधिक तुलना।

    Example:

    Ram is the tallest boy in the class.

  • ---

    • More Examples

    smart

    smarter

    smartest

    good

    better

    best

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    सभी adjectives degree नहीं बनाते।

  • ---

    • Adjective Order

    (विशेषणों का क्रम)

    English में कई adjectives एक साथ आने पर उनका एक सामान्य क्रम होता है।

  • ---

    • Example

    a beautiful small red car

  • ---

    • सामान्य क्रम

    Opinion → Size → Color → Noun

  • ---

    • Example Breakdown

    beautiful → opinion

    small → size

    red → color

    car → noun

  • ---

    • Adjective vs Adverb

    Adjective

    noun/pronoun को modify करता है।

    Example:

    He is a smart boy.

  • ---

    • Adverb

    verb/adjective/adverb को modify करता है।

    Example:

    He runs quickly.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Adjective: “कैसा?”

    Adverb: “कैसे?”

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern grammar में:

    determiner

    article

    quantifier

    numeral

    को कई scholars adjective family का हिस्सा मानते हैं।

    आगे grammar में इसे detail में पढ़ेंगे।

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    कुछ students:

    adjective और adverb को confuse कर देते हैं।

    noun की जगह verb को modify कर देते हैं।

  • ---

    • Tiny Practice

    बताइए नीचे दिए गए adjectives किस प्रकार के हैं:

    1. beautiful

    2. some

    3. three

    4. this

    5. my

    Part 20 — Modern Adjective Family Expansion

    (आधुनिक विशेषण परिवार विस्तार)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, Part 19 में हमने adjective system पढ़ा।

    अब हम grammar के एक बहुत important modern concept को समझेंगे।

    पुराने समय में:

    article

    determiner

    quantifier

    numeral

    को adjective family के अंदर ही पढ़ाया जाता था।

    लेकिन modern grammar में: इनकी अलग विशेषताओं और अलग rules की वजह से इन्हें अलग पहचान दी गई।

  • ---

    • Important Historical Understanding

    पुराने समय में adjective एक बहुत बड़ा परिवार था।

    उसके अंदर:

    determiner

    article

    quantifier

    numeral

    सब शामिल थे।

    लेकिन आधुनिक grammar scholars ने देखा कि: इनका function और grammar rules अलग हैं।

    इसलिए: इन्हें अलग categories की तरह पढ़ाना अधिक सही माना गया।

  • ---

    • Modern Adjective Family

    1. Determiner

    2. Article

    3. Quantifier

    4. Numeral

  • ---

    • 1. Determiner

    (निर्धारक)

    English Definition

    A word that comes before a noun to identify it or point it out is called a determiner.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वह शब्द जो noun से पहले आकर उसे पहचानने या उसकी ओर संकेत करने का कार्य करे, determiner कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    this boy

    that house

    these books

    those students

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Determiner: noun की सीमा तय करता है।

    यह बताता है:

    कौन-सा noun

    किस noun की बात हो रही है

  • ---

    • Important Rule

    Determiner सामान्यतः noun से पहले आता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    this book

    my pen

    those boys

  • ---

    • Determiner vs Adjective

    Adjective

    quality बताता है।

    Examples:

    red car

    smart boy

  • ---

    • Determiner

    noun की पहचान/सीमा बताता है।

    Examples:

    this book

    that girl

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Adjective

    कैसा?

  • ---

    • Determiner

    कौन-सा?

  • ---

    • Why Modern Grammar Separated Determiners

    क्योंकि: determiners के rules adjectives से अलग हैं।

  • ---

    • Rule 1 — Degree Rule

    Adjective: degree बदल सकता है।

    Examples:

    smart

    smarter

    smartest

  • ---

    • लेकिन determiner: degree नहीं बदलता।

    ❌ thiser

    ❌ thisest

  • ---

    • Rule 2 — Position Rule

    Determiner सामान्यतः सबसे पहले आता है।

    Example:

    this beautiful girl

  • ---

    • यहाँ: this → determiner

    beautiful → adjective

  • ---

    • Rule 3 — Repetition Rule

    एक noun के साथ: कई adjectives आ सकते हैं।

    Example:

    a tall handsome smart boy

  • ---

    • लेकिन: दो determiners सामान्यतः साथ नहीं आते।

    ❌ the this boy

    ❌ a my book

  • ---

    • 2. Article

    (आर्टिकल)

    English Definition

    An article is a word that comes before a noun to indicate whether the noun is general or specific.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    Article वह शब्द है जो noun से पहले आकर यह बताता है कि noun सामान्य है या विशेष।

  • ---

    • Types of Articles

    1. Indefinite Articles

    a

    an

  • ---

    • 2. Definite Article

    the

  • ---

    • Use of “A”

    “A” का प्रयोग singular countable noun से पहले होता है जो consonant sound से शुरू हो।

  • ---

    • Examples

    a boy

    a cat

    a university

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    university: vowel letter से शुरू है, लेकिन sound: “यु”

    आ रही है।

    इसलिए: a university

  • ---

    • Use of “An”

    “An” का प्रयोग singular countable noun से पहले होता है जो vowel sound से शुरू हो।

  • ---

    • Examples

    an apple

    an egg

    an honest man

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    honest: “H” silent है।

    इसलिए: an honest man

  • ---

    • Definite Article “The”

    “The” specific noun को दिखाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    the sun

    the moon

    the Taj Mahal

  • ---

    • General vs Specific

    a girl

    → कोई भी लड़की

    the girl

    → कोई विशेष लड़की

  • ---

    • Pronunciation of “The”

    “The” = द

    जब अगला word consonant sound से शुरू हो।

    Example:

    the boy

    the Hindu

  • ---

    • “The” = दी

    जब अगला word vowel sound से शुरू हो।

    Example:

    the elephant

    the apple

  • ---

    • Article vs Adjective

    Similarity

    दोनों noun के बारे में information देते हैं।

  • ---

    • Difference

    Adjective

    noun की quality बताता है।

    Example:

    smart boy

  • ---

    • Article

    noun general है या specific, यह बताता है।

    Example:

    a boy

    the boy

  • ---

    • Important Rule

    अगर article और adjective दोनों हों, तो article पहले आएगा।

  • ---

    • Example

    a tall boy ✅

    ❌ tall a boy

  • ---

    • 3. Quantifier

    (परिमाण बोधक)

    English Definition

    A quantifier is a word that indicates the amount or quantity of a noun in an indefinite way.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो शब्द किसी noun की मात्रा का बोध कराए लेकिन exact संख्या न बताए, उसे quantifier कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    some water

    many books

    few students

    much milk

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Quantifier: exact counting नहीं देता, सिर्फ quantity का अंदाज़ा देता है।

  • ---

    • Quantifier vs Numeral

    Quantifier

    approximate quantity

    Examples:

    some

    many

    few

  • ---

    • Numeral

    exact number/order

    Examples:

    one

    two

    first

    second

  • ---

    • 4. Numeral

    (संख्या बोधक)

    English Definition

    A numeral is a word that indicates the exact number or order of a noun.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो शब्द किसी noun की सही संख्या या क्रम का बोध कराए, उसे numeral कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Types of Numeral

    Cardinal Numeral

    Quantity बताता है।

    Examples:

    one

    two

    three

  • ---

    • Ordinal Numeral

    Position बताता है।

    Examples:

    first

    second

    third

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Quantifier: अंदाज़ा

    Numeral: exact counting

  • ---

    • Old Grammar vs Modern Grammar

    Old Grammar

    सब adjective family के अंदर थे।

  • ---

    • Modern Grammar

    अब:

    determiner

    article

    quantifier

    numeral

    को अलग functional categories माना जाता है।

  • ---

    • Why?

    क्योंकि:

    इनके grammar rules अलग हैं

    sentence position अलग है

    usage logic अलग है

  • ---

    • Easy Family Logic

    पुराने समय में: adjective एक बड़ा परिवार था।

    अब: उसके कुछ “बच्चों” को modern grammar ने अलग पहचान दे दी।

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ the this boy

    ❌ a my book

  • ---

    • ✅ this smart boy

    ✅ a tall girl

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern linguistics में: determiners को कई बार adjective से भी अलग माना जाता है।

    लेकिन traditional grammar में: इन्हें adjective family से जोड़कर पढ़ाया जाता है।

    दोनों systems को समझना जरूरी है।

    Part 21 — Verb System

    (क्रिया प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    noun

    pronoun

    adjective

    समझा।

    अब हम grammar के सबसे महत्वपूर्ण parts में से एक: Verb समझेंगे।

    क्योंकि: verb के बिना सामान्यतः sentence complete नहीं होता।

    Verb:

    action

    state

    happening

    को व्यक्त करता है।

  • ---

    • What is a Verb?

    English Definition

    The word that expresses an action or a state of being is called a verb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वह शब्द जो किसी कार्य, अवस्था या घटना को बताए, verb कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    run → दौड़ना

    eat → खाना

    write → लिखना

    think → सोचना

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Verb केवल physical action नहीं बताता।

    यह:

    मानसिक क्रिया

    अवस्था

    अस्तित्व

    भी बता सकता है।

  • ---

    • Types of Verb According to Function

    1. Action Verb

    2. State Verb

  • ---

    • 1. Action Verb

    (कार्यवाचक क्रिया)

    English Definition

    The verb that expresses an action is called an action verb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb किसी कार्य या क्रिया का बोध कराए, उसे Action Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Physical Actions

    run → दौड़ना

    eat → खाना

    beat → मारना

    write → लिखना

  • ---

    • Mental Actions

    think → सोचना

    understand → समझना

    remember → याद रखना

    believe → विश्वास करना

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    He runs fast.

    → वह तेज दौड़ता है।

    I understand the lesson.

    → मैं पाठ समझता हूँ।

  • ---

    • 2. State Verb

    (अवस्थावाचक क्रिया)

    English Definition

    The verb that expresses a state or condition is called a state verb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb किसी अवस्था या स्थिति का बोध कराए, उसे State Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    am

    is

    are

    was

    were

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    He is a boy.

    → वह लड़का है।

    She is happy.

    → वह खुश है।

    I am a teacher.

    → मैं शिक्षक हूँ।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    इन sentences में: कोई action नहीं हो रहा।

    Verb: स्थिति/अवस्था बता रहा है।

  • ---

    • Main Verb

    (मुख्य क्रिया)

    English Definition

    The main verb is the principal verb that expresses the main action or state in a sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb sentence का मुख्य कार्य या मुख्य अवस्था बताए, उसे Main Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    He plays cricket.

    यहाँ: plays = main verb

  • ---

    • She is singing.

    यहाँ: singing = main verb

  • ---

    • Helping Verb / Auxiliary Verb

    (सहायक क्रिया)

    English Definition

    The verb that helps the main verb to form tense, voice, mood, or question is called a helping verb or auxiliary verb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb मुख्य क्रिया की सहायता करे, उसे Helping Verb या Auxiliary Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    am

    is

    are

    was

    were

    do

    does

    did

    have

    has

    had

    will

    shall

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    She is singing.

    is → helping verb

    singing → main verb

  • ---

    • I have completed my work.

    have → helping verb

    completed → main verb

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Helping verb:

    tense बनाने में

    question बनाने में

    negative sentence बनाने में

    मदद करता है।

  • ---

    • Verb Forms

    (क्रिया के रूप)

    English verbs सामान्यतः पाँच forms में पढ़े जाते हैं।

  • ---

    • V1 — Base Form

    go

    eat

    write

  • ---

    • V2 — Past Form

    went

    ate

    wrote

  • ---

    • V3 — Past Participle

    gone

    eaten

    written

  • ---

    • V4 — ING Form

    going

    eating

    writing

  • ---

    • V5 — S/ES Form

    goes

    eats

    writes

  • ---

    • Example Table

    V1V2V3V4V5

    gowentgonegoinggoes

    eatateeateneatingeats

    writewrotewrittenwritingwrites

  • ---

    • Finite Verb

    (निश्चित क्रिया)

    English Definition

    A finite verb is a verb that changes according to tense, number, or person.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb tense, number या person के अनुसार बदलती है, उसे Finite Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    He goes to school.

    They go to school.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    यहाँ: go/goes

    subject के अनुसार बदल रहा है।

    इसलिए: finite verb

  • ---

    • Non-Finite Verb

    (अनिश्चित क्रिया)

    English Definition

    A non-finite verb is a verb that does not change according to tense, number, or person.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb tense, number या person के अनुसार नहीं बदलती, उसे Non-Finite Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    To read is good.

    Reading is useful.

    He likes to swim.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    यहाँ: to read

    reading

    to swim

    subject या tense के अनुसार नहीं बदल रहे।

  • ---

    • Transitive Verb

    (सकर्मक क्रिया)

    English Definition

    The verb that requires an object to complete its meaning is called a transitive verb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb अपना अर्थ पूरा करने के लिए object माँगे, उसे Transitive Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    He eats mangoes.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    eats → verb

    mangoes → object

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    अगर object हटाएँ:

    He eats…

    sentence अधूरा लगता है।

  • ---

    • Intransitive Verb

    (अकर्मक क्रिया)

    English Definition

    The verb that does not require an object to complete its meaning is called an intransitive verb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो verb अपना अर्थ पूरा करने के लिए object न माँगे, उसे Intransitive Verb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    The baby cried.

    Birds fly.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    यहाँ: कोई object आवश्यक नहीं है।

  • ---

    • Subject-Verb Agreement

    Verb को: subject के number और person के अनुसार बदलना पड़ता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    He goes to school. ✅

    They go to school. ✅

  • ---

    • He go to school. ❌

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Singular Subject

    → singular verb

  • ---

    • Plural Subject

    → plural verb

  • ---

    • Be Verb System

    Present

    am

    is

    are

  • ---

    • Past

    was

    were

  • ---

    • Future

    shall be

    will be

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    I am ready.

    She is happy.

    They are students.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Be verbs: अक्सर अवस्था, पहचान या स्थिति बताते हैं।

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ He go to school.

    ✅ He goes to school.

  • ---

    • ❌ They is happy.

    ✅ They are happy.

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern grammar में:

    gerund

    participle

    infinitive

    को verb family का विस्तार माना जाता है।

    आगे grammar में इन्हें detail में पढ़ेंगे।

    Part 22 — Verb Family Expansion

    (क्रिया परिवार विस्तार)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, Part 21 में हमने:

    main verb

    helping verb

    action/state verb

    transitive/intransitive

    finite/non-finite

    समझा।

    अब हम verb family के advanced members को समझेंगे।

    पुराने grammar system में: इन सबको सामान्य verb के अंदर ही पढ़ाया जाता था।

    लेकिन modern grammar में: इनके अलग functions की वजह से इन्हें अलग पहचान दी गई।

  • ---

    • Verb Family Expansion

    1. Gerund

    2. Participle

    3. Infinitive

  • ---

    • Important Historical Understanding

    पुराने समय में: verb एक बहुत बड़ा परिवार था।

    लेकिन modern grammar ने देखा कि: कुछ verbs:

    noun की तरह

    adjective की तरह

    special structure की तरह

    काम कर रहे हैं।

    इसलिए: उन्हें अलग categories दी गई।

  • ---

    • 1. Gerund

    (क्रियार्थक संज्ञा)

    English Definition

    When the “ing” form of a verb is used like a noun in a sentence, it is called a gerund.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जब verb के “ing” form का प्रयोग sentence में noun की तरह किया जाए, उसे gerund कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Basic Formula

    Verb + ing

    acting like noun

  • ---

    • Examples

    Swimming is my hobby.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    swimming

    → verb का ing form

    लेकिन यहाँ: यह noun की तरह काम कर रहा है।

    क्यों?

    क्योंकि: यह hobby का नाम बन गया है।

  • ---

    • More Examples

    Reading is useful.

    → पढ़ना उपयोगी है।

    Walking is good for health.

    → चलना स्वास्थ्य के लिए अच्छा है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Gerund: काम भी दिखाता है, और noun की तरह भी काम करता है।

  • ---

    • Verb vs Gerund

    Verb

    I am swimming.

    यहाँ: swimming = action verb

  • ---

    • Gerund

    Swimming is my hobby.

    यहाँ: swimming = noun

  • ---

    • Final Easy Rule

    अगर: verb noun की तरह काम करे, तो gerund।

  • ---

    • 2. Participle

    (क्रियात्मक विशेषण)

    English Definition

    A participle is a form of verb that functions as an adjective to describe a noun or pronoun.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    Participle क्रिया का वह रूप है जिसका प्रयोग adjective की तरह noun या pronoun की विशेषता बताने के लिए किया जाता है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Participle: verb से बना होता है, लेकिन काम adjective का करता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    The tired man slept.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    tired

    → verb form से बना

    लेकिन यहाँ: man की विशेषता बता रहा है।

    इसलिए: participle

  • ---

    • More Examples

    A running train

    → दौड़ती हुई ट्रेन

    The broken chair

    → टूटी हुई कुर्सी

    The crying baby

    → रोता हुआ बच्चा

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Participle: noun की condition/quality/action state बताता है।

  • ---

    • Participle vs Adjective

    Adjective

    smart boy

  • ---

    • Participle

    running boy

  • ---

    • Difference

    Adjective: सीधा quality बताता है।

    Participle: verb से बनकर quality बताता है।

  • ---

    • Types of Participle

    Present Participle

    Verb + ing

    Examples:

    running

    crying

    swimming

  • ---

    • Past Participle

    V3 form

    Examples:

    broken

    written

    tired

  • ---

    • 3. Infinitive

    (क्रिया का मूल रूप)

    English Definition

    An infinitive is the base form of a verb usually preceded by “to”.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    Verb का मूल रूप जो सामान्यतः “to” के साथ प्रयोग किया जाए, infinitive कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Basic Formula

    to + verb

  • ---

    • Examples

    to go

    to eat

    to read

    to write

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    I want to play.

    She likes to sing.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    to play

    to sing

    infinitive हैं।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Infinitive: verb का special form है।

    यह:

    noun

    adjective

    adverb

    की तरह भी काम कर सकता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Noun Function

    To read is good.

  • ---

    • Adjective Function

    I need a book to read.

  • ---

    • Adverb Function

    He came to help me.

  • ---

    • Gerund vs Participle vs Infinitive

    FormMain Function

    GerundVerb acting as noun

    ParticipleVerb acting as adjective

    InfinitiveTo + verb special structure

  • ---

    • Easy Family Logic

    पुराने समय में: ये सब verb family के अंदर थे।

    Modern grammar ने: इनके अलग-अलग functions देखकर इन्हें अलग नाम दे दिए।

  • ---

    • Verbal Noun

    (क्रियार्थक संज्ञा)

    जब verb noun की तरह काम करे।

    Example:

    Swimming is useful.

  • ---

    • Verbal Adjective

    (क्रियात्मक विशेषण)

    जब verb adjective की तरह काम करे।

    Example:

    a running train

  • ---

    • Non-Finite Verb Awareness

    Gerund, participle और infinitive: तीनों non-finite verb family के सदस्य माने जाते हैं।

    क्योंकि: ये tense/person के अनुसार नहीं बदलते।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Finite Verb

    He goes to school.

  • ---

    • Non-Finite Verb

    Going to school is useful.

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ I enjoy to swim.

    ✅ I enjoy swimming.

  • ---

    • ❌ He is a run boy.

    ✅ He is a running boy.

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern linguistics में: gerund और participle के कुछ forms overlap भी कर सकते हैं।

    लेकिन beginner level पर: function-based understanding सबसे important है।

  • ---

    • Final Easy Rule

    Verb acting like noun

    → gerund

  • ---

    • Verb acting like adjective

    → participle

  • ---

    • To + verb structure

    → infinitive

    Part 23 — Adverb System Deep Study

    (क्रिया-विशेषण प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, Part 19 में हमने adjective पढ़ा था।

    अब हम adverb को detail में समझेंगे।

    कई students:

    adjective और

    adverb

    को confuse कर देते हैं।

    लेकिन: इन दोनों का काम अलग होता है।

  • ---

    • What is an Adverb?

    English Definition

    The word that describes a verb, adjective, or another adverb is called an adverb.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वह शब्द जो किसी verb, adjective या दूसरे adverb की विशेषता बताए, उसे adverb कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Adjective

    noun/pronoun को modify करता है।

  • ---

    • Adverb

    verb

    adjective

    दूसरे adverb

    को modify करता है।

  • ---

    • 1. Adverb Modifying a Verb

    Example

    He runs quickly.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    runs

    → verb

    quickly

    → runs को modify कर रहा है।

    इसलिए: quickly = adverb

  • ---

    • More Examples

    She sings beautifully.

    → वह सुंदर गाती है।

    They worked hard.

    → उन्होंने मेहनत से काम किया।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    यहाँ adverb: काम कैसे हुआ, यह बता रहा है।

  • ---

    • 2. Adverb Modifying an Adjective

    Example

    He is very smart.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    smart

    → adjective

    very

    → smart को modify कर रहा है।

    इसलिए: very = adverb

  • ---

    • More Examples

    She is extremely beautiful.

    This question is too difficult.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    यहाँ adverb: adjective की intensity बढ़ा रहा है।

  • ---

    • 3. Adverb Modifying Another Adverb

    Example

    He runs very quickly.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    quickly

    → adverb

    very

    → quickly को modify कर रहा है।

    इसलिए: very भी adverb है।

  • ---

    • More Examples

    She speaks quite softly.

    They worked very carefully.

  • ---

    • Final Easy Rule

    Verb को modify करे

    → adverb

  • ---

    • Adjective को modify करे

    → adverb

  • ---

    • दूसरे adverb को modify करे

    → adverb

  • ---

    • Common Ending of Adverbs

    अधिकतर adverbs: “ly” से समाप्त होते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    slowly

    quickly

    beautifully

    carefully

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    लेकिन: सभी adverbs “ly” वाले नहीं होते।

  • ---

    • Examples

    fast

    hard

    late

    well

  • ---

    • Types of Adverb

    अब हम adverb के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

  • ---

    • 1. Adverb of Manner

    (रीतिवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adverb that tells how an action happens is called an adverb of manner.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कैसे हुआ, उसे Adverb of Manner कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    slowly

    quickly

    carefully

    beautifully

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    The boy writes neatly.

    She danced beautifully.

  • ---

    • Question Trick

    How?

  • ---

    • Example

    How does he write?

    Answer: neatly

  • ---

    • 2. Adverb of Time

    (कालवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adverb that tells when an action happens is called an adverb of time.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कब हुआ, उसे Adverb of Time कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    today

    tomorrow

    yesterday

    now

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    We will go tomorrow.

    He came yesterday.

  • ---

    • Question Trick

    When?

  • ---

    • Example

    When will we go?

    Answer: tomorrow

  • ---

    • 3. Adverb of Place

    (स्थानवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adverb that tells where an action happens is called an adverb of place.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कहाँ हुआ, उसे Adverb of Place कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    here

    there

    outside

    upstairs

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Please sit here.

    The cat slept upstairs.

  • ---

    • Question Trick

    Where?

  • ---

    • Example

    Where did the cat sleep?

    Answer: upstairs

  • ---

    • 4. Adverb of Frequency

    (आवृत्तिवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adverb that tells how often an action happens is called an adverb of frequency.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो adverb यह बताए कि कार्य कितनी बार होता है, उसे Adverb of Frequency कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    always

    often

    sometimes

    never

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    He always speaks the truth.

    She never drinks tea.

  • ---

    • Question Trick

    How often?

  • ---

    • 5. Adverb of Degree

    (परिमाणवाचक क्रिया-विशेषण)

    English Definition

    The adverb that tells the intensity or degree of something is called an adverb of degree.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो adverb किसी कार्य, गुण या अवस्था की मात्रा या तीव्रता बताए, उसे Adverb of Degree कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    very

    too

    quite

    extremely

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    She is very smart.

    This box is too heavy.

  • ---

    • Adverb Position

    Adverb sentence में अलग-अलग स्थान पर आ सकता है।

  • ---

    • Beginning

    Yesterday, I met him.

  • ---

    • Middle

    He always comes late.

  • ---

    • End

    She sings beautifully.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Adverb की position: उसके type और emphasis पर depend करती है।

  • ---

    • Adjective vs Adverb

    AdjectiveAdverb

    noun/pronoun modify करता हैverb/adjective/adverb modify करता है

    smart boyruns quickly

  • ---

    • Examples

    He is a quick runner.

    → quick = adjective

    He runs quickly.

    → quickly = adverb

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Adjective

    कैसा?

  • ---

    • Adverb

    कैसे? कब? कहाँ? कितनी बार?

  • ---

    • Multiple Adverbs in One Sentence

    Example

    The tired cat slept quietly upstairs.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    quietly

    → कैसे सोया?

    upstairs

    → कहाँ सोया?

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    एक sentence में: एक से अधिक adverbs हो सकते हैं।

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ He runs quick.

    ✅ He runs quickly.

  • ---

    • ❌ She sings beautiful.

    ✅ She sings beautifully.

  • ---

    • Exception Awareness

    कुछ words: adjective और adverb दोनों हो सकते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    fast

    hard

    late

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    He is a fast runner.

    → adjective

    He runs fast.

    → adverb

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern grammar में: कुछ grammarians adverbs को:

    sentence adverb

    focusing adverb

    linking adverb

    जैसी categories में भी बाँटते हैं।

    आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

    Part 24 — Preposition System

    (संबंध बोधक अव्यय प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    noun

    pronoun

    adjective

    verb

    adverb

    समझा।

    अब हम preposition समझेंगे।

    Sentence में केवल words होना काफी नहीं होता।

    उनके बीच:

    relation

    position

    direction

    time

    भी बताना पड़ता है।

    यही काम preposition करता है।

  • ---

    • What is a Preposition?

    English Definition

    A word placed before a noun, pronoun, or noun phrase to show its relation with another part of the sentence is called a preposition.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वह शब्द जो noun, pronoun या noun phrase से पहले आकर उसका संबंध sentence के दूसरे शब्दों से जोड़ता है, preposition कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Preposition: दो words या groups के बीच relation दिखाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    in

    on

    at

    to

    with

    under

    over

    beside

    between

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    The book is on the table.

    Ram is in the room.

    She sat beside me.

  • ---

    • Relation Logic

    Preposition सामान्यतः बताता है:

    कहाँ?

    कब?

    किस दिशा में?

    किसके साथ?

    किसके ऊपर/नीचे?

  • ---

    • Types of Preposition

    अब हम preposition के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

  • ---

    • 1. Preposition of Place

    (स्थान बोधक संबंध)

    English Definition

    The preposition that shows place or position is called a preposition of place.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो preposition किसी स्थान या स्थिति का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Place कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    in

    on

    under

    behind

    beside

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    The cat is under the table.

    The picture is on the wall.

    Ram is in the classroom.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    in

    अंदर

  • ---

    • on

    ऊपर (touching surface)

  • ---

    • under

    नीचे

  • ---

    • 2. Preposition of Time

    (समय बोधक संबंध)

    English Definition

    The preposition that shows time is called a preposition of time.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो preposition समय का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Time कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Main Time Prepositions

    at

    on

    in

  • ---

    • Use of “At”

    Specific time

  • ---

    • Examples

    at 5 o’clock

    at night

  • ---

    • Use of “On”

    Specific day/date

  • ---

    • Examples

    on Monday

    on 15 August

  • ---

    • Use of “In”

    Longer periods

  • ---

    • Examples

    in 2025

    in winter

    in the morning

  • ---

    • Final Easy Rule

    At

    exact time

  • ---

    • On

    day/date

  • ---

    • In

    month/year/long period

  • ---

    • 3. Preposition of Direction

    (दिशा बोधक संबंध)

    English Definition

    The preposition that shows movement or direction is called a preposition of direction.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो preposition दिशा या movement का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Direction कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    to

    towards

    into

    onto

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    He went to school.

    The boy jumped into the river.

    She walked towards the market.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Direction prepositions: movement दिखाते हैं।

  • ---

    • 4. Preposition of Cause or Purpose

    (कारण/उद्देश्य बोधक संबंध)

    English Definition

    The preposition that shows reason or purpose is called a preposition of cause or purpose.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो preposition कारण या उद्देश्य का बोध कराए, उसे Preposition of Cause/Purpose कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    for

    because of

    due to

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    He was punished for his mistake.

    The match was cancelled because of rain.

  • ---

    • Preposition + Noun Phrase

    Preposition सामान्यतः noun phrase के साथ आता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    on the table

    in the classroom

    under the old tree

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Preposition के बाद:

    noun

    pronoun

    noun phrase

    आता है।

  • ---

    • Preposition vs Adverb

    कई बार same word:

    preposition या

    adverb

    दोनों हो सकता है।

  • ---

    • Example 1

    He went inside the room.

    inside + noun

    → preposition

  • ---

    • Example 2

    He went inside.

    noun नहीं है

    → adverb

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Preposition

    के बाद object आता है।

  • ---

    • Adverb

    के बाद object जरूरी नहीं।

  • ---

    • Important Preposition Difference

    In vs Into

    In

    स्थिति

    The boy is in the room.

  • ---

    • Into

    movement अंदर की ओर

    The boy went into the room.

  • ---

    • On vs Onto

    On

    स्थिति

    The book is on the table.

  • ---

    • Onto

    movement ऊपर की ओर

    The cat jumped onto the table.

  • ---

    • Between vs Among

    Between

    दो के बीच

    The ball is between Ram and Mohan.

  • ---

    • Among

    कई लोगों/वस्तुओं के बीच

    He was sitting among friends.

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ He discussed about the issue.

    ✅ He discussed the issue.

  • ---

    • ❌ She entered into the room.

    ✅ She entered the room.

  • ---

    • Fixed Preposition Awareness

    कुछ verbs/adjectives के साथ fixed prepositions आते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    interested in

    good at

    afraid of

    depend on

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    She is interested in music.

    He is good at English.

  • ---

    • Prepositional Phrase

    English Definition

    A group of words beginning with a preposition and ending with its object is called a prepositional phrase.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    शब्दों का वह समूह जो preposition से शुरू होकर उसके object पर समाप्त हो, prepositional phrase कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    in the room

    under the table

    beside the river

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern grammar में: कुछ grammarians prepositions को:

    simple preposition

    compound preposition

    phrase preposition

    में भी बाँटते हैं।

    आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

    Part 25 — Conjunction System

    (समुच्चय बोधक अव्यय प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    noun

    pronoun

    adjective

    verb

    adverb

    preposition

    समझा।

    अब हम conjunction समझेंगे।

    Sentence में कई बार:

    words

    phrases

    clauses

    को जोड़ना पड़ता है।

    यही काम conjunction करता है।

  • ---

    • What is a Conjunction?

    English Definition

    The word that is used to connect words, phrases, or clauses is called a conjunction.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वह शब्द जो दो शब्दों, वाक्यांशों या उपवाक्यों को जोड़ने का कार्य करे, conjunction कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Conjunction: एक bond या connection की तरह काम करता है।

  • ---

    • Connecting Words

    tea and coffee

    Ram and Shyam

  • ---

    • Connecting Phrases

    on the table or under the table

  • ---

    • Connecting Clauses

    I wanted to go, but it was raining.

  • ---

    • Types of Conjunction

    अब हम conjunction के मुख्य प्रकार समझेंगे।

  • ---

    • 1. Coordinating Conjunction

    (समन्वयी समुच्चयबोधक)

    English Definition

    The conjunction that joins words, phrases, or clauses of equal importance is called a coordinating conjunction.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो conjunction समान महत्व वाले words, phrases या clauses को जोड़े, उसे Coordinating Conjunction कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Main Coordinating Conjunctions

    and

    but

    or

    so

    for

    nor

    yet

  • ---

    • Functions of Coordinating Conjunction

    Addition

    and

  • ---

    • Examples

    Ram and Shyam

    Tea and coffee

  • ---

    • Contrast

    but / yet

  • ---

    • Examples

    He is rich but unhappy.

    She is wise yet humble.

  • ---

    • Choice

    or

  • ---

    • Examples

    Tea or coffee

    You can stay or leave.

  • ---

    • Result

    so

  • ---

    • Examples

    It was raining, so we stayed home.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Coordinating conjunction: दो equal level के parts को जोड़ता है।

  • ---

    • 2. Subordinating Conjunction

    (आश्रित समुच्चयबोधक)

    English Definition

    The conjunction that joins a dependent clause to an independent clause is called a subordinating conjunction.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो conjunction dependent clause को independent clause से जोड़े, उसे Subordinating Conjunction कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    because

    if

    when

    although

    since

    while

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    I stayed home because it was raining.

    When the teacher came, the students stood up.

  • ---

    • Clause Understanding

    Independent Clause

    जो अकेले पूरा meaning दे सके।

    Example:

    I stayed home.

  • ---

    • Dependent Clause

    जो अकेले पूरा meaning न दे सके।

    Example:

    because it was raining

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Subordinating conjunction: एक clause को दूसरे पर dependent बनाता है।

  • ---

    • 3. Correlative Conjunction

    (सहसंबंधी समुच्चयबोधक)

    English Definition

    The conjunctions that work in pairs are called correlative conjunctions.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो conjunction जोड़े में कार्य करें, उन्हें Correlative Conjunction कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    either…or

    neither…nor

    both…and

    not only…but also

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Either Ram or Mohan will come.

    Neither the teacher nor the students were ready.

    Both tea and coffee are available.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Correlative conjunction: pair में काम करता है।

  • ---

    • Conjunction vs Preposition

    Conjunction

    clauses/words जोड़ता है।

    Example:

    I was tired but I worked.

  • ---

    • Preposition

    noun/pronoun से relation दिखाता है।

    Example:

    He sat on the chair.

  • ---

    • Conjunction vs Relative Pronoun

    Relative Pronoun

    noun + clause जोड़ता है।

    Example:

    The boy who came here is my friend.

  • ---

    • Conjunction

    दो clauses जोड़ता है।

    Example:

    I came because you called me.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Relative pronoun: noun का relation बनाता है।

    Conjunction: clause connection बनाता है।

  • ---

    • Common Conjunction Functions

    FunctionConjunction

    Additionand

    Contrastbut

    Choiceor

    Causebecause

    Conditionif

    Timewhen

    Resultso

  • ---

    • Multiple Conjunction Example

    Although he was tired, he continued working because he wanted success.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    although

    → contrast

    because

    → cause

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    एक sentence में: एक से अधिक conjunction हो सकते हैं।

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ Because he was ill.

    → incomplete sentence

    ✅ He stayed home because he was ill.

  • ---

    • ❌ Although he is rich but unhappy.

    ✅ Although he is rich, he is unhappy.

    ✅ He is rich but unhappy.

  • ---

    • Conjunction and Sentence Building

    Conjunction: simple sentences को:

    longer

    smoother

    logical

    बनाता है।

  • ---

    • Example

    Simple

    Ram came. Mohan came.

  • ---

    • With Conjunction

    Ram and Mohan came.

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern grammar में: कुछ conjunctions को:

    coordinating markers

    subordinators

    discourse connectors

    जैसे नामों से भी पढ़ाया जाता है।

    आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

    Part 26 — Interjection System

    (विस्मयादिबोधक प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    noun

    pronoun

    adjective

    verb

    adverb

    preposition

    conjunction

    समझा।

    अब हम interjection समझेंगे।

    English में कई बार:

    खुशी

    दुख

    दर्द

    आश्चर्य

    गुस्सा

    डर

    जैसी अचानक भावनाएँ व्यक्त करनी पड़ती हैं।

    इन्हें व्यक्त करने के लिए: interjection का प्रयोग किया जाता है।

  • ---

    • What is an Interjection?

    English Definition

    A word or phrase used to express sudden emotion without adding grammatical meaning to the sentence is called an interjection.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वह शब्द या शब्द समूह जो अचानक उत्पन्न भावना या आवेग को व्यक्त करे, लेकिन sentence में कोई grammatical meaning न जोड़े, interjection कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Interjection: grammar structure का मुख्य भाग नहीं होता।

    यह: speaker की feeling/emotion दिखाता है।

  • ---

    • Common Emotions Expressed by Interjection

    joy

    surprise

    pain

    sorrow

    anger

    greeting

    approval

    disgust

  • ---

    • 1. Interjection of Joy

    (खुशी)

    Examples

    Hurray!

    Hurrah!

    Wow!

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Hurray! We won the match.

    Wow! This is amazing.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    यहाँ: interjection अचानक खुशी व्यक्त कर रहा है।

  • ---

    • 2. Interjection of Surprise

    (आश्चर्य)

    Examples

    Oh!

    Wow!

    What!

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Wow! What a beautiful house!

    Oh! I did not know that.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    यहाँ: speaker की surprise दिखाई जा रही है।

  • ---

    • 3. Interjection of Pain

    (दर्द)

    Examples

    Ouch!

    Ah!

    Alas!

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Ouch! The pin pricked me.

    Ah! My leg hurts.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    यहाँ: interjection अचानक दर्द व्यक्त कर रहा है।

  • ---

    • 4. Interjection of Sorrow

    (दुःख)

    Examples

    Alas!

    Oh no!

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Alas! He is dead.

    Oh no! We lost the game.

  • ---

    • Explanation

    यहाँ: दुःख या अफसोस व्यक्त हो रहा है।

  • ---

    • 5. Interjection of Greeting

    (अभिवादन)

    Examples

    Hello!

    Hi!

    Good morning!

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Hello! How are you?

    Good morning! Students.

  • ---

    • 6. Interjection of Approval

    (प्रशंसा/स्वीकृति)

    Examples

    Bravo!

    Excellent!

  • ---

    • Example Sentences

    Bravo! You did well.

    Excellent! Your answer is correct.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Interjection: sentence के बाकी grammar structure से अलग भी खड़ा हो सकता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Wow!

    Amazing!

    Oops!

  • ---

    • Interjection and Punctuation

    Interjection के बाद सामान्यतः: exclamation mark (!)

    लगाया जाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Hurray!

    Ouch!

    Wow!

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Exclamation mark: strong emotion दिखाता है।

  • ---

    • Interjection vs Normal Sentence

    Interjection

    Wow!

  • ---

    • Normal Sentence

    This house is very beautiful.

  • ---

    • Difference

    Interjection: emotion directly व्यक्त करता है।

    Normal sentence: complete information देता है।

  • ---

    • Interjection in Spoken English

    Spoken English में: interjections communication को:

    natural

    expressive

    emotional

    बनाते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Oops! I forgot my book.

    Hey! Listen to me.

    Well! Let us start.

  • ---

    • Common Mistakes

    ❌ Hurray we won the match

    ✅ Hurray! We won the match.

  • ---

    • ❌ Wow what a beautiful place

    ✅ Wow! What a beautiful place!

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Interjection: sentence में meaning add नहीं करता, लेकिन emotion add करता है।

  • ---

    • Small Advanced Awareness

    Modern grammar में: कुछ grammarians interjections को:

    discourse marker

    emotional marker

    conversational expression

    की तरह भी study करते हैं।

    आगे advanced grammar में इसकी awareness मिलेगी।

    Part 27 — Number, Person, Agreement & Sentence Drill System

    (वचन, पुरुष, सामंजस्य एवं वाक्य अभ्यास प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    noun

    pronoun

    adjective

    verb

    adverb

    preposition

    conjunction

    interjection

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम grammar के उस भाग में प्रवेश कर रहे हैं जहाँ:

    sentence बनाना

    translation करना

    spoken English शुरू करना

    वास्तविक रूप से शुरू होगा।

    यह भाग: grammar और spoken English के बीच का bridge है।

  • ---

    • Number System

    (वचन प्रणाली)

    English Definition

    The counting of things is called number.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    वस्तुओं की गिनती को number या वचन कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Types of Number

    1. Singular Number

    2. Plural Number

  • ---

    • Singular Number

    (एकवचन)

    English Definition

    The noun that refers to one person, place, thing, idea, or quality is called singular number.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो noun एक व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का बोध कराए, उसे singular number कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    boy

    girl

    book

    apple

  • ---

    • Plural Number

    (बहुवचन)

    English Definition

    The noun that refers to more than one person, place, thing, idea, or quality is called plural number.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो noun एक से अधिक व्यक्ति, स्थान, वस्तु, विचार या गुण का बोध कराए, उसे plural number कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    boys

    girls

    books

    apples

  • ---

    • Person System

    (पुरुष प्रणाली)

    Sentence में:

    बोलने वाला

    सुनने वाला

    जिसके बारे में बात हो रही है

    इनके आधार पर person तय होता है।

  • ---

    • Types of Person

    1. First Person

    2. Second Person

    3. Third Person

  • ---

    • First Person

    (उत्तम पुरुष)

    जो बोलता है।

    Examples:

    I

    We

  • ---

    • Second Person

    (मध्यम पुरुष)

    जिससे बात की जाए।

    Example:

    You

  • ---

    • Third Person

    (अन्य पुरुष)

    जिसके बारे में बात की जाए।

    Examples:

    He

    She

    It

    They

    Ram

  • ---

    • Subject-Verb Agreement

    (कर्ता-क्रिया सामंजस्य)

    English Definition

    The verb must agree with its subject in number and person.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    Verb को अपने subject के number और person के अनुसार बदलना पड़ता है।

  • ---

    • Present Form Agreement

    SubjectVerb

    I/We/You/Theygo

    He/She/Itgoes

  • ---

    • Examples

    I go to school.

    He goes to school.

    We play cricket.

    She plays cricket.

  • ---

    • Past Form Agreement

    Past form सामान्यतः सभी subjects के साथ same रहती है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    I went to school.

    He went to school.

    They went to school.

  • ---

    • Be Verb System

    Present Form

    SubjectBe Verb

    Iam

    He/She/Itis

    We/You/Theyare

  • ---

    • Examples

    I am happy.

    He is ready.

    They are students.

  • ---

    • Past Form

    SubjectBe Verb

    I/He/She/Itwas

    We/You/Theywere

  • ---

    • Examples

    She was absent.

    They were tired.

  • ---

    • Future Form

    SubjectBe Verb

    I/Weshall be / will be

    He/She/It/You/Theywill be

  • ---

    • Examples

    I shall be ready.

    He will be happy.

    They will be successful.

  • ---

    • Helping Verb System

    Present

    do

    does

    have

    has

  • ---

    • Past

    did

    had

  • ---

    • Examples

    I do my work.

    He does his homework.

    She has a car.

    They had a meeting.

  • ---

    • Sentence Forms

    (वाक्य के प्रकार)

  • ---

    • 1. Affirmative Sentence

    (सकारात्मक वाक्य)

    English Definition

    A sentence that makes a positive statement is called an affirmative sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो वाक्य सामान्य सकारात्मक कथन दे, उसे affirmative sentence कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    I am happy.

    He plays cricket.

    They are students.

  • ---

    • 2. Negative Sentence

    (नकारात्मक वाक्य)

    English Definition

    A sentence that expresses negation is called a negative sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो वाक्य निषेध या इंकार व्यक्त करे, उसे negative sentence कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    I am not happy.

    He does not play cricket.

    They are not students.

  • ---

    • 3. Interrogative Sentence

    (प्रश्नवाचक वाक्य)

    English Definition

    A sentence that asks a question is called an interrogative sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो वाक्य प्रश्न पूछे, उसे interrogative sentence कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Am I happy?

    Does he play cricket?

    Are they students?

  • ---

    • 4. Interrogative Negative Sentence

    (नकारात्मक प्रश्नवाचक वाक्य)

    English Definition

    A sentence that is both interrogative and negative is called an interrogative negative sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो वाक्य प्रश्न और निषेध दोनों व्यक्त करे, उसे interrogative negative sentence कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Am I not happy?

    Does he not play cricket?

    Are they not students?

  • ---

    • Short Answer System

    Examples

    Are you ready?

    → Yes, I am.

    → No, I am not.

  • ---

    • Is he happy?

    → Yes, he is.

    → No, he is not.

  • ---

    • Contracted Forms

    (Short Spoken Forms)

    Examples

    I am → I’m

    He is → He’s

    They are → They’re

    do not → don’t

    does not → doesn’t

    is not → isn’t

    are not → aren’t

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Contracted forms: spoken English को natural बनाते हैं।

  • ---

    • Basic Translation Drill System

    अब हम एक ही pattern से: सैकड़ों sentences बनाना सीखेंगे।

  • ---

    • Pattern 1 — “Good”

    Affirmative

    I am good.

    मैं अच्छा हूँ।

    We are good.

    हम अच्छे हैं।

    You are good.

    तुम अच्छे हो।

    He is good.

    वह अच्छा है।

    She is good.

    वह अच्छी है।

    It is good.

    यह अच्छा है।

    They are good.

    वे अच्छे हैं।

  • ---

    • Negative

    I am not good.

    मैं अच्छा नहीं हूँ।

    We are not good.

    हम अच्छे नहीं हैं।

    He is not good.

    वह अच्छा नहीं है।

    She is not good.

    वह अच्छी नहीं है।

    They are not good.

    वे अच्छे नहीं हैं।

  • ---

    • Interrogative

    Am I good?

    क्या मैं अच्छा हूँ?

    Are we good?

    क्या हम अच्छे हैं?

    Are you good?

    क्या तुम अच्छे हो?

    Is he good?

    क्या वह अच्छा है?

    Is she good?

    क्या वह अच्छी है?

    Are they good?

    क्या वे अच्छे हैं?

  • ---

    • Interrogative Negative

    Am I not good?

    क्या मैं अच्छा नहीं हूँ?

    Is he not good?

    क्या वह अच्छा नहीं है?

    Are they not good?

    क्या वे अच्छे नहीं हैं?

  • ---

    • WH Question System

    What

    → क्या

    What are you doing?

  • ---

    • Who

    → कौन

    Who are you?

  • ---

    • When

    → कब

    When will you come?

  • ---

    • Where

    → कहाँ

    Where do you live?

  • ---

    • Why

    → क्यों

    Why are you sad?

  • ---

    • How

    → कैसे

    How are you?

  • ---

    • Which

    → कौन-सा

    Which book is yours?

  • ---

    • Whose

    → किसका

    Whose pen is this?

  • ---

    • Whom

    → किसे / किसको

    Whom did you call?

  • ---

    • WH Pattern Drill

    How am I good?

    मैं कैसे अच्छा हूँ?

    How are we good?

    हम कैसे अच्छे हैं?

    How are you good?

    तुम कैसे अच्छे हो?

    How is he good?

    वह कैसे अच्छा है?

    How is she good?

    वह कैसे अच्छी है?

    How are they good?

    वे कैसे अच्छे हैं?

  • ---

    • WH Negative Drill

    Why am I not ready?

    मैं तैयार क्यों नहीं हूँ?

    How is she not happy?

    वह खुश क्यों नहीं है?

    Why are they not present?

    वे उपस्थित क्यों नहीं हैं?

  • ---

    • Substitution Drill System

    अब एक ही pattern में word बदलकर सैकड़ों sentence बनाए जाएँगे।

  • ---

    • Example Words

    good

    bad

    happy

    sad

    ready

    busy

    hungry

    tired

  • ---

    • Examples

    I am happy.

    He is busy.

    They are tired.

  • ---

    • Daily Use Sentence Bank

    Emotion

    I am happy.

    She is sad.

  • ---

    • Need

    I need water.

    He needs help.

  • ---

    • Ability

    I can swim.

    She can dance.

  • ---

    • Basic Command & Request

    Come here.

    Sit down.

    Please help me.

  • ---

    • Basic Modal Verb Awareness

    can

    may

    should

    must

  • ---

    • Examples

    I can swim.

    You should study.

    We must work hard.

  • ---

    • Word Order Rule

    English में सामान्य word order:

    Subject + Verb + Object

  • ---

    • Examples

    I play cricket.

    She reads books.

  • ---

    • Wrong vs Right

    ❌ I good am.

    ✅ I am good.

  • ---

    • ❌ He go to school.

    ✅ He goes to school.

  • ---

    • ❌ Does he goes?

    ✅ Does he go?

  • ---

    • Mini Conversation Drill

    How are you?

    → I am fine.

    Where do you live?

    → I live in Patna.

    What do you do?

    → I am a teacher.

  • ---

    • Vocabulary Integration Strategy

    अब vocabulary को अलग से नहीं, patterns के अंदर सिखाया जाएगा।

  • ---

    • Example Vocabulary Group

    Emotion Words

    happy

    sad

    angry

    tired

  • ---

    • Pattern

    I am happy.

    She is tired.

    They are angry.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    जब vocabulary: grammar patterns में repeatedly use होती है, तो:

    जल्दी याद होती है

    speaking में automatically आने लगती है

    translation आसान हो जाता है।

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 27

    Student:

    sentence बनाना शुरू करे

    grammar को apply करे

    translation करे

    spoken English शुरू करे

    patterns को पहचानकर नए sentences बना सके।

    Part 28 — Sentence Construction & Spoken Drill System

    (वाक्य निर्माण एवं बोलचाल अभ्यास प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    parts of speech

    verb system

    agreement system

    helping verb

    WH words

    sentence forms

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम grammar को वास्तविक English में बदलेंगे।

    यही वह भाग है जहाँ: student को पहली बार लगेगा:

    “Yes, I can speak English.”

  • ---

    • What is a Sentence?

    English Definition

    A group of words that expresses a complete thought is called a sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    शब्दों का ऐसा समूह जो पूरा अर्थ दे, sentence कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Examples

    I am ready.

    मैं तैयार हूँ।

    She is happy.

    वह खुश है।

    They play cricket.

    वे क्रिकेट खेलते हैं।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Sentence में सामान्यतः:

    subject

    verb

    जरूरी होते हैं।

  • ---

    • Basic Sentence Formula

    Subject + Verb + Object

  • ---

    • Examples

    I play cricket.

    She reads books.

    They eat mangoes.

  • ---

    • Spoken Drill System

    अब हम: एक ही structure को:

    person

    number

    tense

    question

    negative

    में घुमाकर practice करेंगे।

    इसे: Pattern Rotation Drill कहेंगे।

  • ---

    • Pattern 1 — “Go”

    Present Affirmative

    I go.

    मैं जाता हूँ।

    We go.

    हम जाते हैं।

    You go.

    तुम जाते हो।

    He goes.

    वह जाता है।

    She goes.

    वह जाती है।

    It goes.

    यह जाता है।

    They go.

    वे जाते हैं।

  • ---

    • Present Negative

    I do not go.

    मैं नहीं जाता हूँ।

    We do not go.

    हम नहीं जाते हैं।

    He does not go.

    वह नहीं जाता है।

    She does not go.

    वह नहीं जाती है।

    They do not go.

    वे नहीं जाते हैं।

  • ---

    • Present Interrogative

    Do I go?

    क्या मैं जाता हूँ?

    Do we go?

    क्या हम जाते हैं?

    Do you go?

    क्या तुम जाते हो?

    Does he go?

    क्या वह जाता है?

    Does she go?

    क्या वह जाती है?

    Do they go?

    क्या वे जाते हैं?

  • ---

    • Present Interrogative Negative

    Do I not go?

    क्या मैं नहीं जाता हूँ?

    Does he not go?

    क्या वह नहीं जाता है?

    Do they not go?

    क्या वे नहीं जाते हैं?

  • ---

    • WH Question Drill

    Why do I go?

    मैं क्यों जाता हूँ?

    Where does he go?

    वह कहाँ जाता है?

    When do they go?

    वे कब जाते हैं?

    How does she go?

    वह कैसे जाती है?

  • ---

    • WH Negative Drill

    Why do I not go?

    मैं क्यों नहीं जाता हूँ?

    Why does he not go?

    वह क्यों नहीं जाता है?

  • ---

    • Pattern 2 — “Good”

    Present Affirmative

    I am good.

    मैं अच्छा हूँ।

    We are good.

    हम अच्छे हैं।

    You are good.

    तुम अच्छे हो।

    He is good.

    वह अच्छा है।

    She is good.

    वह अच्छी है।

    It is good.

    यह अच्छा है।

    They are good.

    वे अच्छे हैं।

  • ---

    • Negative

    I am not good.

    He is not good.

    They are not good.

  • ---

    • Interrogative

    Am I good?

    Is he good?

    Are they good?

  • ---

    • Interrogative Negative

    Am I not good?

    Is she not good?

    Are they not good?

  • ---

    • WH Drill

    How am I good?

    Why is he good?

    Where are they good?

  • ---

    • Past Pattern Drill

    “Go”

    I went.

    मैं गया।

    He went.

    वह गया।

    They went.

    वे गए।

  • ---

    • Negative

    I did not go.

    He did not go.

    They did not go.

  • ---

    • Interrogative

    Did I go?

    Did he go?

    Did they go?

  • ---

    • Past Be Verb Pattern

    I was ready.

    He was happy.

    They were busy.

  • ---

    • Future Pattern Drill

    I shall go.

    He will go.

    They will go.

  • ---

    • Negative

    I shall not go.

    He will not go.

  • ---

    • Interrogative

    Shall I go?

    Will he go?

    Will they go?

  • ---

    • Future Be Verb Pattern

    I shall be ready.

    He will be successful.

    They will be happy.

  • ---

    • Massive Substitution Drill

    अब: एक ही structure में: word बदलकर सैकड़ों sentence बनाए जाएँगे।

  • ---

    • Example Vocabulary

    happy

    sad

    busy

    ready

    hungry

    tired

    angry

  • ---

    • Pattern

    I am happy.

    He is busy.

    They are tired.

  • ---

    • Verb Rotation Drill

    play

    eat

    write

    read

    run

    sing

  • ---

    • Examples

    I play.

    He plays.

    They play.

  • ---

    • Negative

    I do not play.

    He does not play.

  • ---

    • Question

    Do you play?

    Does he play?

  • ---

    • Daily Life Sentence Drill

    Emotion

    I am sad.

    She is angry.

  • ---

    • Need

    I need water.

    He needs money.

  • ---

    • Ability

    I can swim.

    She can dance.

  • ---

    • Possession

    I have a pen.

    They have books.

  • ---

    • Spoken English Mini Conversation

    Greeting

    How are you?

    → I am fine.

  • ---

    • Identity

    What is your name?

    → My name is Ram.

  • ---

    • Place

    Where do you live?

    → I live in Patna.

  • ---

    • Work

    What do you do?

    → I am a teacher.

  • ---

    • Command Sentence

    (आज्ञासूचक वाक्य)

    English Definition

    A sentence that expresses command, order, advice, or request is called an imperative sentence.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    जो वाक्य आदेश, अनुरोध, सलाह या निर्देश दे, उसे imperative sentence कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Sit down.

    Come here.

    Please help me.

    Study hard.

  • ---

    • Modal Verb Spoken Drill

    can

    may

    should

    must

  • ---

    • Examples

    I can swim.

    You should study.

    We must work hard.

    May I come in?

  • ---

    • Short Answer System

    Are you ready?

    → Yes, I am.

    → No, I am not.

  • ---

    • Do you play cricket?

    → Yes, I do.

    → No, I do not.

  • ---

    • Contracted Forms

    I am → I’m

    He is → He’s

    They are → They’re

    do not → don’t

    does not → doesn’t

    will not → won’t

  • ---

    • Error Detection System

    ❌ He go to school.

    ✅ He goes to school.

  • ---

    • ❌ Does he goes?

    ✅ Does he go?

  • ---

    • ❌ I good am.

    ✅ I am good.

  • ---

    • Vocabulary Integration System

    अब vocabulary को: sentence pattern के अंदर याद कराया जाएगा।

  • ---

    • Example

    happy

    sad

    hungry

    busy

  • ---

    • Pattern Practice

    I am happy.

    She is busy.

    They are hungry.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    जब vocabulary: grammar pattern के अंदर repeatedly use होती है, तो:

    जल्दी याद होती है

    बोलने में आने लगती है

    translation आसान हो जाता है।

    Student:

    English sentence बना सके

    बोल सके

    translation कर सके

    WH question बना सके

    real conversation शुरू कर सके

    grammar को practically use कर सके।

    • Latest Strategic Suggestions

    1. Add “Memory Revision Blocks”

    After every 3–4 parts: add:

    recap drill

    mixed translation

    rapid-fire correction

    This prevents overload.

  • ---

    • 2. Add “Mistake Psychology”

    Example:

    ❌ He go

    ✅ He goes

    Explain: WHY brain creates this mistake.

    This is extremely powerful.

  • ---

    • 3. Add “Hindi Thinking Trap”

    Example:

    मैं अच्छा हूँ

    NOT: ❌ I good am

    Explain: Hindi order vs English order.

    Very important for Hindi-medium learners.

  • ---

    • 4. Add “Speaking Speed Layers”

    Level 1: slow pattern

    Level 2: normal

    Level 3: fast spoken repetition

    This will dramatically improve fluency.

    Instead of random words.

    Example:

    School Cluster

    teacher student classroom homework exam

    Then sentence drill.

    This is much stronger psychologically.

    • 6. Add “Micro Conversation Engine”

    Tiny real conversations after each chapter.

    Example:

    Where do you live?

    I live in Patna.

    What do you do?

    I am a teacher.

    This creates practical confidence early.

    Tense Frequency Priority System

    Do NOT teach all tenses equally.

    Teach:

    real spoken tenses first

    low-frequency tenses later

    This is a major modern teaching advantage.
