    • यह addition आपके पूरे grammar system को: normal grammar book से उठाकर real English mastery system बना देगा।

    Part 31A — Spoken Communication System

    (व्यावहारिक बोलचाल अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    grammar

    tense

    sentence structure

    translation

    advanced grammar

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम: Real Spoken English सीखेंगे।

    यह भाग:

    बोलने

    समझने

    प्रतिक्रिया देने

    बातचीत करने

    के लिए बनाया गया है।

  • ---

    • Main Goal of Part 31A

    Student:

    डर हटाए

    तुरंत sentence बना सके

    daily English बोल सके

    real communication कर सके

  • ---

    • Included Systems

    1. Daily Spoken Patterns

    2. Introduction System

    3. Question-Answer System

    4. Real-Life Conversation System

    5. Functional English System

    6. Expression System

    7. Confidence Drill System

  • ---

    • 1. Daily Spoken Patterns

    (दैनिक बोलचाल पैटर्न)

  • ---

    • Basic Patterns

    I am ready.

    मैं तैयार हूँ।

    I am busy.

    मैं व्यस्त हूँ।

    I am tired.

    मैं थका हुआ हूँ।

    I am hungry.

    मुझे भूख लगी है।

    I am feeling cold.

    मुझे ठंड लग रही है।

  • ---

    • Daily Action Patterns

    I am going home.

    मैं घर जा रहा हूँ।

    I am studying English.

    मैं अंग्रेज़ी पढ़ रहा हूँ।

    I am waiting for you.

    मैं तुम्हारा इंतजार कर रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Habit Patterns

    I wake up early.

    मैं जल्दी उठता हूँ।

    I go to school daily.

    मैं रोज़ स्कूल जाता हूँ।

    I drink tea every morning.

    मैं हर सुबह चाय पीता हूँ।

  • ---

    • Ability Patterns

    I can swim.

    मैं तैर सकता हूँ।

    She can speak English.

    वह अंग्रेज़ी बोल सकती है।

    They can help us.

    वे हमारी मदद कर सकते हैं।

  • ---

    • 2. Introduction System

    (परिचय प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Self Introduction

    My name is Ram.

    मेरा नाम राम है।

    I am from Bihar.

    मैं बिहार से हूँ।

    I am a teacher.

    मैं एक शिक्षक हूँ।

    I live in Patna.

    मैं पटना में रहता हूँ।

  • ---

    • Asking Introduction

    What is your name?

    तुम्हारा नाम क्या है?

    Where are you from?

    तुम कहाँ से हो?

    What do you do?

    तुम क्या करते हो?

  • ---

    • Response Practice

    I am a student.

    मैं एक विद्यार्थी हूँ।

    I work in a school.

    मैं एक विद्यालय में काम करता हूँ।

  • ---

    • 3. Question-Answer System

    (प्रश्न-उत्तर प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Yes/No Questions

    Do you play cricket?

    क्या तुम क्रिकेट खेलते हो?

    Yes, I do.

    हाँ, मैं खेलता हूँ।

    No, I do not.

    नहीं, मैं नहीं खेलता।

  • ---

    • WH Questions

    Where do you live?

    तुम कहाँ रहते हो?

    I live in Delhi.

    मैं दिल्ली में रहता हूँ।

  • ---

    • Why are you late?

    तुम देर से क्यों आए?

    Because I missed the bus.

    क्योंकि मेरी बस छूट गई।

  • ---

    • Daily Question Practice

    What are you doing?

    तुम क्या कर रहे हो?

    I am studying English.

    मैं अंग्रेज़ी पढ़ रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • When will you come?

    तुम कब आओगे?

    I will come tomorrow.

    मैं कल आऊँगा।

  • ---

    • 4. Real-Life Conversation System

    (वास्तविक जीवन वार्तालाप प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • In Classroom

    May I come in, sir?

    क्या मैं अंदर आ सकता हूँ, सर?

    Yes, come in.

    हाँ, अंदर आओ।

    Please sit down.

    कृपया बैठ जाओ।

  • ---

    • At Shop

    How much is this?

    यह कितने का है?

    It is five hundred rupees.

    यह पाँच सौ रुपये का है।

  • ---

    • Can you reduce the price?

    क्या आप कीमत कम कर सकते हैं?

  • ---

    • On Phone

    Hello, who is speaking?

    हैलो, कौन बोल रहा है?

    Please call me later.

    कृपया मुझे बाद में कॉल करें।

  • ---

    • Asking for Help

    Can you help me?

    क्या आप मेरी मदद कर सकते हैं?

    Sure, I will help you.

    ज़रूर, मैं आपकी मदद करूँगा।

  • ---

    • 5. Functional English System

    (कार्यात्मक अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Request

    Please help me.

    कृपया मेरी मदद करें।

    Please open the door.

    कृपया दरवाजा खोलिए।

  • ---

    • Permission

    May I sit here?

    क्या मैं यहाँ बैठ सकता हूँ?

    May I use your pen?

    क्या मैं आपका पेन उपयोग कर सकता हूँ?

  • ---

    • Suggestion

    You should study hard.

    तुम्हें मेहनत से पढ़ना चाहिए।

    We should leave now.

    हमें अब निकलना चाहिए।

  • ---

    • Advice

    Do not waste your time.

    अपना समय बर्बाद मत करो।

    Always speak the truth.

    हमेशा सच बोलो।

  • ---

    • Obligation

    You must obey your parents.

    तुम्हें अपने माता-पिता की बात माननी चाहिए।

    Students must complete homework.

    विद्यार्थियों को गृहकार्य पूरा करना चाहिए।

  • ---

    • 6. Expression System

    (भाव अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Happiness

    I am very happy today.

    मैं आज बहुत खुश हूँ।

    That is wonderful.

    यह बहुत शानदार है।

  • ---

    • Sadness

    I am feeling sad.

    मैं दुखी महसूस कर रहा हूँ।

    That is very unfortunate.

    यह बहुत दुर्भाग्यपूर्ण है।

  • ---

    • Surprise

    Really?

    सच में?

    That is amazing!

    यह अद्भुत है!

  • ---

    • Anger

    Do not disturb me.

    मुझे परेशान मत करो।

    I am very angry right now.

    मैं अभी बहुत गुस्से में हूँ।

  • ---

    • Politeness

    Thank you very much.

    बहुत धन्यवाद।

    You are welcome.

    आपका स्वागत है।

    Sorry for the mistake.

    गलती के लिए क्षमा करें।

  • ---

    • 7. Confidence Drill System

    (आत्मविश्वास अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Single Pattern Rotation

    I am ready.

    मैं तैयार हूँ।

    We are ready.

    हम तैयार हैं।

    He is ready.

    वह तैयार है।

    They are ready.

    वे तैयार हैं।

  • ---

    • Negative Rotation

    I am not ready.

    मैं तैयार नहीं हूँ।

    He is not ready.

    वह तैयार नहीं है।

  • ---

    • Interrogative Rotation

    Are you ready?

    क्या तुम तैयार हो?

    Is he ready?

    क्या वह तैयार है?

  • ---

    • WH Rotation

    Why are you ready?

    तुम तैयार क्यों हो?

    Why is he angry?

    वह गुस्से में क्यों है?

  • ---

    • Spoken Speed Drill

    Slow → Normal → Fast

  • ---

    • Example

    I am ready.

    I am ready.

    I’m ready.

  • ---

    • Common Spoken Contractions

    I am → I’m

    He is → He’s

    They are → They’re

    Do not → Don’t

    Will not → Won’t

    Cannot → Can’t

  • ---

    • Real Spoken Understanding

    Formal English: I am going home.

    Natural Spoken English: I’m going home.

  • ---

    • Mini Conversation Drill

    Conversation 1

    A: What are you doing?

    तुम क्या कर रहे हो?

    B: I am studying English.

    मैं अंग्रेज़ी पढ़ रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Conversation 2

    A: Where do you live?

    तुम कहाँ रहते हो?

    B: I live in Patna.

    मैं पटना में रहता हूँ।

  • ---

    • Conversation 3

    A: Can you help me?

    क्या आप मेरी मदद कर सकते हैं?

    B: Yes, of course.

    हाँ, बिल्कुल।

  • ---

    • Most Important Understanding

    Spoken English: grammar + confidence + repetition का combination है।

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 31A

    Student:

    daily English बोल सके

    conversation कर सके

    तुरंत जवाब दे सके

    real-life communication कर सके

    hesitation कम कर सके

    English में सोचना शुरू कर सके।

    Part 31B — Translation Intelligence & English Thinking System

    (अनुवाद बुद्धिमत्ता एवं अंग्रेज़ी सोच प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, translation का मतलब केवल Hindi sentence को English sentence में बदलना नहीं है।

    Real translation का मतलब है:

    meaning transfer

    context understanding

    natural expression

    English thinking

    situation awareness

    समझना।

    यही कारण है कि कभी grammar सही होने पर भी sentence awkward लगता है, और कभी शब्द बदलने पर भी meaning पूरी तरह गलत हो जाती है।

  • ---

    • Main Goal of Part 31B

    Student:

    word-by-word translation से बाहर निकले

    Hindi-thinking mistakes पहचान सके

    contextual English समझ सके

    natural English बोल सके

    awkward English से बच सके

    English expression system समझ सके

    different verbs and expressions का सही use सीख सके

  • ---

    • Included Systems in Part 31B

    1. Direct Translation System

    2. Raw Literal Translation System

    3. Grammatical Literal Translation System

    4. Contextual Translation System

    5. Natural English Translation System

    6. Translation Psychology System

    7. Hindi vs English Thinking System

    8. Similar Verb Difference System

    9. Figurative Hindi Expression System

    10. Indian English vs Global English System

    11. Environment-Based Translation System

    12. Real-Life Translation Drill System

  • ---

    • 1. Direct Translation System

    (प्रत्यक्ष अनुवाद प्रणाली)

    English Definition

    Direct translation means translating a sentence directly from one language into another language.

    Hindi Definition

    जब किसी वाक्य का सीधे दूसरी भाषा में अनुवाद किया जाए, उसे direct translation कहते हैं।

    Important Understanding

    Direct translation कभी सही होता है, कभी गलत।

    Simple factual sentences में यह अक्सर ठीक काम करता है।

    Examples

    राम स्कूल जाता है।

    ✅ Ram goes to school.

    मैं किताब पढ़ रहा हूँ।

    ✅ I am reading a book.

  • ---

    • 2. Raw Literal Translation System

    (कच्चा शब्दशः अनुवाद)

    English Definition

    Raw literal translation means translating every word directly without caring about grammar, context, or natural expression.

    Hindi Definition

    जब grammar, context और natural usage की चिंता किए बिना हर शब्द का सीधा अनुवाद किया जाए, उसे raw literal translation कहते हैं।

    Examples

    सड़क पर गोलियाँ चल रही हैं।

    ❌ Bullets are walking on the road.

    वहाँ पानी ही पानी था।

    ❌ There was water water.

    उसने मेरी नाक में दम कर दिया।

    ❌ He filled breath in my nose.

    Literal Hindi Meaning of These Wrong English Lines

    Bullets are walking on the road.

    → गोलियाँ सड़क पर चल रही हैं।

    There was water water.

    → वहाँ पानी पानी था।

    He filled breath in my nose.

    → उसने मेरी नाक में साँस भर दी।

    Important Understanding

    Raw literal translation language psychology समझने के लिए useful है, लेकिन real English नहीं होता।

  • ---

    • 3. Grammatical Literal Translation System

    (व्याकरणिक शब्दशः अनुवाद)

    English Definition

    Grammatical literal translation follows grammar rules but may still sound unnatural.

    Hindi Definition

    जब grammar सही हो लेकिन expression natural न लगे, उसे grammatical literal translation कहते हैं।

    Examples

    सड़क पर गोलियाँ चल रही हैं।

    ⚠️ Bullets are moving on the road.

    वहाँ पानी ही पानी था।

    ⚠️ There was only water.

    मेरी बस छूट गई।

    ⚠️ The bus left without me.

    Why Weak?

    Grammar ठीक है

    लेकिन English natural नहीं लग रहा

    Hindi expression का real feeling नहीं आ रहा

  • ---

    • 4. Contextual Translation System

    (संदर्भगत अनुवाद प्रणाली)

    English Definition

    Contextual translation translates meaning according to the situation and context rather than exact words.

    Hindi Definition

    जब शब्दों के बजाय परिस्थिति, अर्थ और context के अनुसार अनुवाद किया जाए, उसे contextual translation कहते हैं।

    Examples

    सड़क पर गोलियाँ चल रही हैं।

    ✅ There is firing on the road.

    ✅ Gunfire is going on in the street.

    ✅ Gunfire erupted in the street.

    वहाँ पानी ही पानी था।

    ✅ There was water everywhere.

    ✅ There was nothing but water.

    मेरी बस छूट गई।

    ✅ I missed my bus.

    Important Understanding

    Translation:

    शब्द बदलना नहीं

    meaning transfer करना है

  • ---

    • 5. Natural English Translation System

    (प्राकृतिक अंग्रेज़ी अनुवाद प्रणाली)

    English Definition

    Natural English translation focuses on how native speakers naturally express the idea.

    Hindi Definition

    जब translation native speakers के natural expression के अनुसार किया जाए, उसे natural English translation कहते हैं।

    Examples

    मुझे ठंड लग रही है।

    ❌ Cold is feeling to me.

    ✅ I am feeling cold.

    ✅ I feel cold.

    मुझे नींद आ रही है।

    ❌ Sleep is coming to me.

    ✅ I am feeling sleepy.

    ✅ I feel sleepy.

    मुझे डर लग रहा है।

    ❌ Fear is feeling to me.

    ✅ I am feeling scared.

    ✅ I feel scared.

    Important Understanding

    Natural English: Hindi copy नहीं करती।

  • ---

    • 6. Translation Psychology System

    (अनुवाद मनोविज्ञान प्रणाली)

    Common Problems

    Hindi-medium learner अक्सर:

    word-by-word सोचता है

    Hindi structure copy करता है

    dictionary meaning directly use करता है

    wrong verb चुनता है

    literal logic पर अटक जाता है

    Example

    उसने मेरी नाक में दम कर दिया।

    ❌ He filled breath in my nose.

    ✅ He irritated me a lot.

    ✅ He troubled me badly.

    Important Understanding

    हर language का:

    अपना culture

    अपना logic

    अपना expression system

    होता है।

  • ---

    • 7. Hindi vs English Thinking System

    (हिंदी एवं अंग्रेज़ी सोच प्रणाली)

    Hindi Structure

    Subject + Object + Verb

    Example

    मैं चाय पीता हूँ।

    मैं → subject

    चाय → object

    पीता हूँ → verb

    English Structure

    Subject + Verb + Object

    Example

    I drink tea.

    I → subject

    drink → verb

    tea → object

    Important Understanding

    Hindi: SOV Structure

    English: SVO Structure

  • ---

    • 8. Similar Verb Difference System

    (समान क्रियाओं का अंतर प्रणाली)

    A. Learn vs Study

    Learn

    skill acquire करना

    I am learning English.

    मैं English सीख रहा हूँ।

    Study

    किसी subject को पढ़ना

    I am studying English grammar.

    मैं English grammar पढ़ रहा हूँ।

    Important Difference

    You can study without learning.

    तुम पढ़ सकते हो, लेकिन सीखना जरूरी नहीं।

  • ---

    • B. Drink Tea / Have Tea / Take Tea

    I drink tea.

    ✅ Modern global English

    ✅ Direct spoken usage

    ✅ Most common and simple

    मैं चाय पीता हूँ।

    I have tea.

    ✅ Very natural daily conversation

    मैं चाय पीता / लेता हूँ।

    I take tea.

    ⚠️ Traditional / formal / polite / old-style expression

    ⚠️ Some British/Indian contexts में used हो सकता है

    मैं चाय लेता हूँ।

    Important Difference

    ExpressionUsage

    I drink teadirect modern global usage

    I have teamost natural daily conversation

    I take teaformal/traditional/polite usage

    Important Understanding

    English में drink का अर्थ: liquid consume करना होता है।

    इसलिए “I drink tea” गलत नहीं है। यह बिल्कुल सही और natural है।

  • ---

    • C. Hear vs Listen

    Hear

    automatic hearing

    I heard a noise.

    मैंने आवाज सुनी।

    Listen

    attention देकर सुनना

    Listen to me carefully.

    ध्यान से मेरी बात सुनो।

  • ---

    • D. See vs Look vs Watch

    See

    अपने आप दिखाई देना

    I can see a bird.

    मैं एक पक्षी देख सकता हूँ।

    Look

    जानबूझकर देखना

    Look at the board.

    बोर्ड की ओर देखो।

    Watch

    लगातार ध्यान से देखना

    We are watching television.

    हम टेलीविजन देख रहे हैं।

  • ---

    • E. Say vs Tell

    Say

    कुछ कहना

    He said something.

    उसने कुछ कहा।

    Tell

    किसी को कुछ बताना

    He told me the truth.

    उसने मुझे सच बताया।

  • ---

    • F. Bring vs Take

    Bring

    speaker की ओर लाना

    Bring me a glass of water.

    मेरे लिए एक गिलास पानी लाओ।

    Take

    speaker से दूर ले जाना

    Take this bag to the room.

    यह बैग कमरे में ले जाओ।

  • ---

    • 9. Figurative Hindi Expression System

    (लाक्षणिक हिंदी अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

    What is Figurative Expression?

    ऐसे expressions जिनका अर्थ सीधे शब्दों से नहीं निकलता।

    Examples

    1

    वहाँ पानी ही पानी था।

    Raw Literal: ❌ There was water water.

    Better Contextual: ✅ There was water everywhere.

    More Intense/Complete: ✅ There was nothing but water.

    2

    उसने मेरी नाक में दम कर दिया।

    Raw Literal: ❌ He filled breath in my nose.

    Natural English: ✅ He irritated me badly.

    Natural English: ✅ He troubled me a lot.

    3

    जान पर बन आई।

    Raw Literal: ❌ It came on life.

    Natural English: ✅ Life was in danger.

    4

    उसकी आँखों में आँसू भर आए।

    Raw Literal: ❌ Tears filled in his eyes.

    Better English: ✅ His eyes filled with tears.

    Important Understanding

    Idiomatic Hindi: directly translate नहीं होती।

  • ---

    • 10. Indian English vs Global English System

    (भारतीय अंग्रेज़ी एवं वैश्विक अंग्रेज़ी)

    Examples

    ❌ He expired.

    ✅ He died.

    ❌ I am having two brothers.

    ✅ I have two brothers.

    ❌ Discuss about this topic.

    ✅ Discuss this topic.

    ❌ Return back.

    ✅ Return.

    ❌ Revert back.

    ✅ Reply.

    Important Understanding

    कुछ expressions Indian English में common हैं, लेकिन global natural English में awkward या गलत माने जाते हैं।

  • ---

    • 11. Environment-Based Translation System

    (परिस्थिति-आधारित अनुवाद प्रणाली)

    एक ही Hindi sentence के अलग-अलग English versions हो सकते हैं, context के अनुसार।

    Example

    सड़क पर गोलियाँ चल रही हैं।

    Spoken English

    ✅ There is firing on the road.

    News English

    ✅ Gunfire erupted in the street.

    Formal Reporting English

    ✅ Gunshots were being fired in the area.

    Emotional English

    ✅ The whole street echoed with gunfire.

    Important Understanding

    एक ही sentence: situation के अनुसार अलग English ले सकता है।

  • ---

    • 12. Real-Life Translation Drill System

    (वास्तविक जीवन अनुवाद अभ्यास)

    Daily Sentences

    मैं घर जा रहा हूँ।

    ✅ I am going home.

    मैं तुम्हारा इंतजार कर रहा हूँ।

    ✅ I am waiting for you.

    वह स्कूल नहीं गया।

    ✅ He did not go to school.

    क्या तुम मुझे जानते हो?

    ✅ Do you know me?

    मैं दो घंटे से पढ़ रहा हूँ।

    ✅ I have been studying for two hours.

    पुलिस के आने से पहले चोर भाग चुका था।

    ✅ The thief had escaped before the police arrived.

    जब मैं घर पहुँचा, मेरी माँ खाना बना रही थी।

    ✅ When I reached home, my mother was cooking food.

  • ---

    • Final Translation Intelligence Formula

    Grammar

    +

    Meaning

    +

    Context

    +

    Natural Usage

    +

    English Thinking

    +

    Situation Awareness

    Real English Translation

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 31B

    Student:

    direct और contextual translation का अंतर समझ सके

    raw literal गलती पहचान सके

    natural English सोच सके

    real-life translation कर सके

    awkward English से बच सके

    similar verbs का सही use सीख सके

    Hindi-thinking mistakes सुधार सके

    global English बोल सके

  • ---

    • One-Page Smart Memory Core

    Translation Levels

    1. Direct Translation

    2. Raw Literal Translation

    3. Grammatical Literal Translation

    4. Contextual Translation

    5. Natural English Translation

    Most Important Rule

    Translation = meaning transfer

    Not just word replacement

    Most Important Habit

    पहले meaning सोचो, फिर English बनाओ

    Most Important Outcome

    Student Hindi से English copy नहीं करेगा, बल्कि English में सोचना शुरू करेगा।

    Part 31C — Real-Life English Application System

    (वास्तविक जीवन अंग्रेज़ी प्रयोग प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    grammar

    tense

    spoken English

    translation intelligence

    English thinking

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम सीखेंगे:

    Real-Life English Application

    यानी: असली जीवन में English कैसे उपयोग होती है।

    यह भाग:

    communication

    social interaction

    practical English

    real environment English

    के लिए बनाया गया है।

  • ---

    • Main Goal of Part 31C

    Student:

    real-life English use कर सके

    situation के अनुसार English बदल सके

    formal और informal English समझ सके

    practical communication कर सके

    environment-based English बोल सके

  • ---

    • Included Systems

    1. Formal vs Informal English

    2. Social English System

    3. Phone Conversation System

    4. Public Place English System

    5. Emotion-Based English System

    6. Politeness & Respect System

    7. Reaction English System

    8. Survival English System

    9. Conversation Expansion System

    10. Real-Life Situation Drill System

  • ---

    • 1. Formal vs Informal English

    (औपचारिक एवं अनौपचारिक अंग्रेज़ी)

  • ---

    • Informal English

    दोस्तों, परिवार या close लोगों के साथ।

  • ---

    • Examples

    What’s up?

    क्या हाल है?

    I’m fine.

    मैं ठीक हूँ।

    See you later.

    फिर मिलते हैं।

  • ---

    • Formal English

    teacher, office, interview, stranger आदि के साथ।

  • ---

    • Examples

    How are you doing?

    आप कैसे हैं?

    I am doing well.

    मैं अच्छा हूँ।

    It was nice meeting you.

    आपसे मिलकर अच्छा लगा।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    हर जगह same English नहीं बोली जाती।

    Situation के अनुसार: tone बदलता है।

  • ---

    • 2. Social English System

    (सामाजिक अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Greeting

    Good morning.

    सुप्रभात।

    Good evening.

    शुभ संध्या।

  • ---

    • Welcoming

    Welcome.

    स्वागत है।

    Please come in.

    कृपया अंदर आइए।

  • ---

    • Thanking

    Thank you very much.

    बहुत धन्यवाद।

    I really appreciate it.

    मैं वास्तव में इसकी सराहना करता हूँ।

  • ---

    • Apology

    I am sorry.

    मुझे क्षमा करें।

    Please forgive me.

    कृपया मुझे माफ करें।

  • ---

    • Congratulation

    Congratulations!

    बधाई हो!

    Well done!

    बहुत बढ़िया!

  • ---

    • 3. Phone Conversation System

    (फोन वार्तालाप प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Starting Call

    Hello, who is speaking?

    हैलो, कौन बोल रहे हैं?

    May I speak to Ram?

    क्या मैं राम से बात कर सकता हूँ?

  • ---

    • During Conversation

    Please speak slowly.

    कृपया धीरे बोलिए।

    I cannot hear you properly.

    मैं आपको ठीक से सुन नहीं पा रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Ending Call

    I will call you later.

    मैं आपको बाद में कॉल करूँगा।

    Take care.

    अपना ध्यान रखिए।

  • ---

    • 4. Public Place English System

    (सार्वजनिक स्थान अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • At Shop

    How much is this?

    यह कितने का है?

    Can you reduce the price?

    क्या आप कीमत कम कर सकते हैं?

  • ---

    • At Station

    When will the train arrive?

    ट्रेन कब आएगी?

    Which platform is it on?

    यह किस प्लेटफॉर्म पर है?

  • ---

    • At Restaurant

    May I see the menu?

    क्या मैं menu देख सकता हूँ?

    I would like some tea.

    मुझे चाय चाहिए।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Real-life English: book grammar से अलग feel देती है।

  • ---

    • 5. Emotion-Based English System

    (भाव आधारित अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Happiness

    I am very happy today.

    मैं आज बहुत खुश हूँ।

    That’s wonderful!

    यह बहुत शानदार है!

  • ---

    • Sadness

    I feel very sad.

    मैं बहुत दुखी महसूस कर रहा हूँ।

    That is unfortunate.

    यह दुर्भाग्यपूर्ण है।

  • ---

    • Anger

    I am very angry.

    मैं बहुत गुस्से में हूँ।

    Do not disturb me.

    मुझे परेशान मत करो।

  • ---

    • Fear

    I am scared.

    मैं डरा हुआ हूँ।

    Something feels wrong.

    कुछ गलत लग रहा है।

  • ---

    • Surprise

    Really?

    सच में?

    That’s unbelievable!

    यह अविश्वसनीय है!

  • ---

    • 6. Politeness & Respect System

    (विनम्रता एवं सम्मान प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Request

    Please help me.

    कृपया मेरी मदद करें।

    Could you open the door?

    क्या आप दरवाजा खोल सकते हैं?

  • ---

    • Permission

    May I come in?

    क्या मैं अंदर आ सकता हूँ?

    May I ask a question?

    क्या मैं एक प्रश्न पूछ सकता हूँ?

  • ---

    • Respectful English

    Would you mind sitting here?

    क्या आपको यहाँ बैठने में आपत्ति होगी?

    Could you please repeat that?

    क्या आप कृपया उसे दोहरा सकते हैं?

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    English में: politeness level बहुत महत्वपूर्ण है।

  • ---

    • 7. Reaction English System

    (प्रतिक्रिया अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Agreement

    You are right.

    आप सही हैं।

    I agree with you.

    मैं आपसे सहमत हूँ।

  • ---

    • Disagreement

    I do not think so.

    मैं ऐसा नहीं सोचता।

    I disagree with you.

    मैं आपसे असहमत हूँ।

  • ---

    • Shock

    Oh my God!

    हे भगवान!

    That is shocking!

    यह चौंकाने वाला है!

  • ---

    • Excitement

    Amazing!

    अद्भुत!

    Fantastic!

    शानदार!

  • ---

    • 8. Survival English System

    (जीवनोपयोगी अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Asking Direction

    How can I go to the station?

    मैं स्टेशन कैसे जा सकता हूँ?

  • ---

    • Emergency

    Please help me!

    कृपया मेरी मदद करें!

    Call the police!

    पुलिस को बुलाइए!

  • ---

    • Health

    I am not feeling well.

    मैं अच्छा महसूस नहीं कर रहा हूँ।

    I need a doctor.

    मुझे डॉक्टर चाहिए।

  • ---

    • Travel

    I need a ticket to Delhi.

    मुझे दिल्ली का टिकट चाहिए।

    Where is the bus stop?

    बस स्टॉप कहाँ है?

  • ---

    • 9. Conversation Expansion System

    (वार्तालाप विस्तार प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Short Answer

    Yes.

  • ---

    • Better Answer

    Yes, I do.

  • ---

    • More Natural Answer

    Yes, I usually do that in the evening.

  • ---

    • Example

    Do you drink tea?

  • ---

    • Basic Answer

    Yes.

  • ---

    • Better Answer

    Yes, I drink tea.

  • ---

    • Expanded Answer

    Yes, I usually have tea in the morning with my family.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Real conversation: single-word answer से आगे बढ़ती है।

  • ---

    • 10. Real-Life Situation Drill System

    (वास्तविक परिस्थिति अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Situation 1 — Asking Help

    Excuse me, can you help me?

    माफ कीजिए, क्या आप मेरी मदद कर सकते हैं?

    Yes, what happened?

    हाँ, क्या हुआ?

  • ---

    • Situation 2 — At School

    May I come in, sir?

    क्या मैं अंदर आ सकता हूँ, सर?

    Yes, come in.

    हाँ, अंदर आओ।

  • ---

    • Situation 3 — At Market

    How much is this shirt?

    यह शर्ट कितने की है?

    It is five hundred rupees.

    यह पाँच सौ रुपये की है।

  • ---

    • Situation 4 — On Phone

    Hello, who is speaking?

    हैलो, कौन बोल रहे हैं?

    This is Ram speaking.

    मैं राम बोल रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Situation 5 — Emergency

    Please help me!

    कृपया मेरी मदद करें!

    What happened?

    क्या हुआ?

  • ---

    • Final Real-Life Communication Formula

    Grammar

    +

    Confidence

    +

    Context

    +

    Politeness

    +

    Natural Expression

    Real Communication Ability

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 31C

    Student:

    real-life English बोल सके

    situation-based English समझ सके

    formal/informal difference पहचान सके

    polite communication कर सके

    daily conversation कर सके

    practical English use कर सके

    public interaction में confidence ला सके।

    Part 31D — Error Correction & Natural English Mastery System

    (त्रुटि सुधार एवं प्राकृतिक अंग्रेज़ी निपुणता प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    grammar

    tense

    spoken English

    translation intelligence

    real-life communication

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम सीखेंगे:

    Error Correction & Natural English Mastery

    यानी:

    गलत English पहचानना

    awkward English सुधारना

    natural English बनाना

    native-like expression समझना

    • Main Goal of Part 31D

    Student:

    grammar mistakes पहचान सके

    translation mistakes सुधार सके

    • Included Systems

    3. Natural English Upgrade System

    4. Awkward vs Natural English System

    6. Verb Usage Error System

    8. Real Spoken English Compression System

  • ---

    • 1. Grammar Error Correction System

    (व्याकरण त्रुटि सुधार प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ He do not play cricket.

    ✅ He does not play cricket.

  • ---

    • Why Wrong?

    He/she/it के साथ: does उपयोग होता है।

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ She go to school daily.

    ✅ She goes to school daily.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ I am study English.

    ✅ I am studying English.

  • ---

    • Why Wrong?

    am/is/are के बाद: V4 आता है।

  • ---

    • Example 4

    ❌ They was playing football.

    ✅ They were playing football.

  • ---

    • 2. Translation Error Correction System

    (अनुवाद त्रुटि सुधार प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    मुझे भूख लगी है।

    ❌ Hunger has attached to me.

    ✅ I am hungry.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    मुझे ठंड लग रही है।

    ❌ Cold is feeling to me.

    ✅ I am feeling cold.

    ✅ I feel cold.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    उसने मेरी नाक में दम कर दिया।

    ❌ He filled breath in my nose.

    ✅ He irritated me a lot.

    ✅ He troubled me badly.

  • ---

    • Example 4

    सड़क पर गोलियाँ चल रही हैं।

    ❌ Bullets are walking on the road.

    ⚠️ Bullets are moving on the road.

    ✅ There is firing on the road.

    ✅ Gunfire is going on in the street.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    हर गलत sentence: same level की गलती नहीं होता।

  • ---

    • Error Levels

    TypeMeaning

    Raw Literal Errorशब्दशः गलती

    Grammar Errorव्याकरण गलती

    Context Errorपरिस्थिति गलती

    Naturalness Errorunnatural English

  • ---

    • 3. Natural English Upgrade System

    (प्राकृतिक अंग्रेज़ी उन्नयन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ⚠️ I drink tea.

    ✅ I have tea.

    ✅ I usually have tea in the evening.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    “I drink tea” गलत नहीं है।

    लेकिन: “I have tea” daily natural conversation में ज्यादा common है।

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ⚠️ I am very tired.

    ✅ I am exhausted.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ⚠️ He is very angry.

    ✅ He is furious.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Natural English: कई बार छोटे simple words की जगह strong natural expressions use करती है।

  • ---

    • 4. Awkward vs Natural English System

    (अस्वाभाविक एवं प्राकृतिक अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ⚠️ The bus left without me.

    ✅ I missed my bus.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ⚠️ Sleep is coming to me.

    ✅ I feel sleepy.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ⚠️ Fear is feeling to me.

    ✅ I feel scared.

  • ---

    • Example 4

    ⚠️ Tears filled in his eyes.

    ✅ His eyes filled with tears.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Grammar सही होने पर भी: sentence awkward हो सकता है।

  • ---

    • 5. Indian English Error System

    (भारतीय अंग्रेज़ी त्रुटि प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ He expired.

    ✅ He died.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ Discuss about this topic.

    ✅ Discuss this topic.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ Return back.

    ✅ Return.

  • ---

    • Example 4

    ❌ Revert back.

    ✅ Reply.

  • ---

    • Example 5

    ❌ I am having two brothers.

    ✅ I have two brothers.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    कुछ expressions: India में common हैं, लेकिन: global English में awkward माने जाते हैं।

  • ---

    • 6. Verb Usage Error System

    (क्रिया प्रयोग त्रुटि प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Learn vs Study

  • ---

    • Wrong Understanding

    ❌ Both are same.

  • ---

    • Correct Understanding

    Learn

    → skill development

    Study

    → subject reading

  • ---

    • Example

    I am learning English.

    मैं English सीख रहा हूँ।

    I am studying English grammar.

    मैं English grammar पढ़ रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Drink vs Have vs Take Tea

  • ---

    • I drink tea.

    ✅ Modern global English

  • ---

    • I have tea.

    ✅ Most natural daily English

  • ---

    • I take tea.

    ⚠️ formal/traditional/British-style usage

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    English verbs: Hindi physical logic से नहीं, native usage pattern से चलते हैं।

  • ---

    • Hear vs Listen

    hear

    → automatic hearing

    listen

    → attention-based hearing

  • ---

    • See vs Look vs Watch

    see

    → naturally visible

    look

    → intentionally see

    watch

    → continuously observe

  • ---

    • 7. Word Order Error System

    (शब्द क्रम त्रुटि प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Hindi Structure

    Subject + Object + Verb

  • ---

    • English Structure

    Subject + Verb + Object

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ I tea drink.

    ✅ I drink tea.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ He English learning is.

    ✅ He is learning English.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ I market going am.

    ✅ I am going to the market.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Hindi word order: English में copy नहीं होता।

  • ---

    • 8. Real Spoken English Compression System

    (वास्तविक बोलचाल संक्षिप्तीकरण प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Formal English

    I am going home.

  • ---

    • Spoken English

    I’m going home.

  • ---

    • Formal English

    Do not worry.

  • ---

    • Spoken English

    Don’t worry.

  • ---

    • Formal English

    I will not do this.

  • ---

    • Spoken English

    I won’t do this.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Native speakers: हर शब्द clearly नहीं बोलते।

  • ---

    • 9. Meaning Confusion System

    (अर्थ भ्रम प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ He is reading in class ten.

    ⚠️ Indian English

    ✅ He studies in class ten.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ Open the light.

    ✅ Turn on the light.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ Close the fan.

    ✅ Turn off the fan.

  • ---

    • Example 4

    ❌ My head is paining.

    ✅ I have a headache.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Dictionary meaning जानना काफी नहीं है।

    Correct usage भी जरूरी है।

  • ---

    • 10. Final Master Correction Drill System

    (अंतिम महारत अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Correct the Sentence

    ❌ He do not know me.

    ✅ He does not know me.

  • ---

    • ❌ I am having a car.

    ✅ I have a car.

  • ---

    • ❌ Bullets are walking on the road.

    ✅ There is firing on the road.

  • ---

    • ❌ Sleep is coming to me.

    ✅ I feel sleepy.

  • ---

    • ❌ I tea drink daily.

    ✅ I drink tea daily.

    ✅ I usually have tea daily.

  • ---

    • Final English Mastery Formula

    Grammar

    +

    Natural Usage

    +

    Context

    +

    Correct Verb Choice

    +

    Word Order

    +

    Native Expression

    Natural English Mastery

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 31D

    Student:

    गलत English पहचान सके

    awkward English सुधार सके

    natural English बना सके

    Indian-English mistakes समझ सके

    native-like expression समझ सके

    confident communication कर सके

    real-world English mastery प्राप्त कर सके।

    big → huge → enormous → gigantic

    angry → upset → annoyed → furious

  • ---

    • क्यों जरूरी?

    क्योंकि: real fluency vocabulary depth से आती है।

  • ---

    • Part 34 — Idiom, Phrase & Expression System

    इसमें आएगा:

    idioms

    phrasal verbs

    native expressions

    figurative English

    conversational phrases

  • ---

    • Example

    Break down

    Give up

    Look after

    Once in a blue moon

    Hit the nail on the head

  • ---

    • क्यों जरूरी?

    क्योंकि: native English idiom-heavy होती है।

    Part 32 — Advanced Spoken & Thinking System

    (उन्नत बोलचाल एवं अंग्रेज़ी सोच प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    grammar

    tense

    translation intelligence

    real-life English

    natural English

    error correction

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम उस स्तर में प्रवेश करेंगे जहाँ:

    English केवल subject नहीं रहेगी, बल्कि: सोचने, प्रतिक्रिया देने, तुरंत बोलने, और real communication का माध्यम बन जाएगी।

  • ---

    • Main Goal of Part 32

    Student:

    English में सोचना शुरू करे

    hesitation हटाए

    fast response देना सीखे

    natural conversation flow समझे

    real spoken English पकड़ सके

    native-style speaking patterns समझ सके

  • ---

    • Included Systems

    1. Thinking in English System

    2. Instant Response System

    3. Conversation Flow System

    4. Filler Word System

    5. Opinion Expression System

    6. Agreement & Disagreement System

    7. Emotional Spoken English System

    8. Real Spoken Compression System

    9. Hesitation Removal Drill System

    10. Advanced Conversation Drill System

  • ---

    • 1. Thinking in English System

    (अंग्रेज़ी में सोच प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Main Problem

    अधिकांश students: पहले Hindi में सोचते हैं, फिर English translate करते हैं।

  • ---

    • Result

    slow speaking

    hesitation

    broken English

    awkward sentence

  • ---

    • Wrong Process

    Hindi Thought

    → Translation

    → English

  • ---

    • Correct Process

    Situation

    → Direct English Thought

    → English Speech

  • ---

    • Example

    तुम क्या कर रहे हो?

  • ---

    • Hindi Thinking Method

    पहले Hindi सोचो

    फिर translate करो

    ⚠️ Slow

  • ---

    • English Thinking Method

    “What am I doing?”

    → I am studying.

    ✅ Fast

  • ---

    • Practice Rule

    छोटी-छोटी चीजें: English में सोचना शुरू करो।

  • ---

    • Examples

    मैं बैठ रहा हूँ।

    → I am sitting.

    मैं पानी पी रहा हूँ।

    → I am drinking water.

    मैं बाजार जा रहा हूँ।

    → I am going to the market.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Thinking speed: spoken fluency की जड़ है।

  • ---

    • 2. Instant Response System

    (तुरंत प्रतिक्रिया प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Goal

    Question सुनते ही: तुरंत reply देना।

  • ---

    • Slow Response Problem

    Student: पहले grammar सोचता है, फिर tense, फिर translation।

  • ---

    • Real Spoken English

    direct response देती है।

  • ---

    • Example

    How are you?

  • ---

    • Weak Response

    ⚠️ I am fine.

  • ---

    • Better Natural Responses

    ✅ I’m doing well.

    ✅ Pretty good.

    ✅ I’m fine, thanks.

  • ---

    • Example

    What are you doing?

  • ---

    • Fast Responses

    ✅ I’m studying.

    ✅ Just relaxing.

    ✅ Working on something.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Real spoken English: fast reaction चाहती है।

  • ---

    • 3. Conversation Flow System

    (वार्तालाप प्रवाह प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Conversation Problem

    Students: one-line answer देकर रुक जाते हैं।

  • ---

    • Weak Conversation

    A: Do you drink tea?

    B: Yes.

    Conversation dead.

  • ---

    • Better Conversation

    A: Do you drink tea?

    B: Yes, I usually have tea in the evening.

  • ---

    • Advanced Flow

    A: Do you drink tea?

    B: Yes, I usually have tea in the evening with my family.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Conversation: single-word answer नहीं है।

    Conversation: flow है।

  • ---

    • 4. Filler Word System

    (वार्तालाप भराव शब्द प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What are Fillers?

    ऐसे शब्द जो: सोचने का समय देते हैं।

  • ---

    • Examples

    Well…

    Actually…

    Honestly…

    Basically…

    You know…

    I mean…

    Let me think…

  • ---

    • Example

    What do you think about English?

  • ---

    • Natural Spoken Reply

    Well, I think English is very important nowadays.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Native speakers भी: हर sentence instantly perfect नहीं बोलते।

  • ---

    • 5. Opinion Expression System

    (मत अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Giving Opinion

    In my opinion…

    मेरे विचार से

    I think…

    मुझे लगता है

    As far as I know…

    जहाँ तक मैं जानता हूँ

    Personally speaking…

    व्यक्तिगत रूप से

  • ---

    • Examples

    I think English is important.

    In my opinion, practice is the key to fluency.

    Personally speaking, spoken English needs confidence.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Opinion English: daily communication का बड़ा हिस्सा है।

  • ---

    • 6. Agreement & Disagreement System

    (सहमति एवं असहमति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Agreement

    I agree with you.

    मैं आपसे सहमत हूँ।

    You are right.

    आप सही हैं।

    Exactly!

    बिल्कुल!

    That’s true.

    यह सही है।

  • ---

    • Soft Disagreement

    I do not think so.

    मैं ऐसा नहीं सोचता।

    Maybe, but…

    शायद, लेकिन…

    I see your point, but…

    मैं आपकी बात समझता हूँ, लेकिन…

  • ---

    • Strong Disagreement

    I completely disagree.

    मैं पूरी तरह असहमत हूँ।

    That is not correct.

    यह सही नहीं है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    English में disagreement भी politely किया जाता है।

  • ---

    • 7. Emotional Spoken English System

    (भावनात्मक बोलचाल अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Excitement

    That’s amazing!

    यह अद्भुत है!

    Awesome!

    शानदार!

  • ---

    • Surprise

    Really?

    सच में?

    No way!

    ऐसा नहीं हो सकता!

  • ---

    • Frustration

    This is so annoying.

    यह बहुत परेशान करने वाला है।

    I am fed up with this.

    मैं इससे तंग आ चुका हूँ।

  • ---

    • Happiness

    I’m really happy today.

    मैं आज बहुत खुश हूँ।

  • ---

    • Sadness

    I feel terrible.

    मैं बहुत बुरा महसूस कर रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Emotion: spoken English को natural बनाता है।

  • ---

    • 8. Real Spoken Compression System

    (वास्तविक बोलचाल संक्षिप्तीकरण प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Formal English

    I am going home.

  • ---

    • Natural Spoken English

    I’m going home.

  • ---

    • Formal English

    Do not worry.

  • ---

    • Spoken English

    Don’t worry.

  • ---

    • Formal English

    I will not do this.

  • ---

    • Spoken English

    I won’t do this.

  • ---

    • Advanced Compression

    Want to

    → wanna

    Going to

    → gonna

    Give me

    → gimme

  • ---

    • Example

    I’m gonna call you later.

    मैं तुम्हें बाद में कॉल करने वाला हूँ।

  • ---

    • Important Note

    यह informal spoken English है, formal writing नहीं।

  • ---

    • 9. Hesitation Removal Drill System

    (हिचकिचाहट हटाने की अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Main Problem

    Student: गलती से डरता है।

  • ---

    • Result

    silence

    hesitation

    slow speaking

  • ---

    • Important Rule

    Broken English

    is better than

    silent fear.

  • ---

    • Practice Method

    एक sentence को:

    slowly

    normally

    fast

    तीनों speed में बोलो।

  • ---

    • Example

    I am learning English.

    I’m learning English.

    I’m learning English every day.

  • ---

    • Daily Thinking Drill

    सुबह उठते ही: English में सोचना शुरू करो।

  • ---

    • Examples

    I need water.

    I am feeling sleepy.

    I have to study today.

  • ---

    • 10. Advanced Conversation Drill System

    (उन्नत वार्तालाप अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Situation 1 — Opinion

    A: What do you think about mobile phones?

    B: Well, I think mobile phones are useful, but overuse is dangerous.

  • ---

    • Situation 2 — Agreement

    A: English is important nowadays.

    B: Yes, I completely agree with you.

  • ---

    • Situation 3 — Disagreement

    A: Grammar is not important.

    B: I do not think so. Grammar is the foundation of language.

  • ---

    • Situation 4 — Emotional Reaction

    A: I passed the exam.

    B: That’s amazing! Congratulations!

  • ---

    • Situation 5 — Instant Response

    A: What are you doing?

    B: Just studying English.

  • ---

    • Final Spoken Intelligence Formula

    Grammar

    +

    Thinking Speed

    +

    Confidence

    +

    Natural Expression

    +

    Instant Response

    +

    Emotion

    Advanced Spoken English

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 32

    Student:

    English में सोचना शुरू करे

    hesitation कम करे

    instant reply दे सके

    natural conversation कर सके

    emotional English समझ सके

    filler words use कर सके

    confidence के साथ बोल सके

    real spoken fluency विकसित कर सके।

    Advanced Vocabulary Intelligence

    Real fluency आती है:

    strong vocabulary

    से।

  • ---

    • 1. Root Word System

    (मूल शब्द प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is Root Word?

    एक ऐसा मूल शब्द जिससे कई नए शब्द बनते हैं।

  • ---

    • Example

    Root: act

    act

    action

    active

    activity

    actor

    activate

    reaction

    interaction

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Root word समझने से: हजारों शब्द जल्दी समझ आते हैं।

  • ---

    • Example

    Root: port

    Meaning: carry करना

  • ---

    • transport

    import

    export

    portable

    report

  • ---

    • Example

    Root: dict

    Meaning: speak

  • ---

    • dictionary

    predict

    dictation

    verdict

  • ---

    • 2. Word Family System

    (शब्द परिवार प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example

    beauty

    beautiful

    beautifully

    beautify

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    एक word family: noun, adjective, adverb, verb सभी forms सिखाती है।

  • ---

    • Another Example

    success

    successful

    successfully

    succeed

  • ---

    • Sentence Usage

    He succeeded in life.

    He is successful.

    He completed the work successfully.

    Success needs discipline.

  • ---

    • 3. Synonym Intelligence System

    (समानार्थी शब्द बुद्धिमत्ता प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Big

    big

    large

    huge

    enormous

    gigantic

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    सबका meaning similar है, लेकिन intensity अलग है।

  • ---

    • Example

    The house is big.

    The building is enormous.

  • ---

    • Another Example

    happy

    glad

    cheerful

    delighted

    ecstatic

  • ---

    • Emotional Intensity Difference

    happy

    → normal happiness

    ecstatic

    → extreme happiness

  • ---

    • 4. Antonym Intelligence System

    (विलोम शब्द बुद्धिमत्ता प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Examples

    happy ↔ sad

    rich ↔ poor

    strong ↔ weak

    victory ↔ defeat

    ancient ↔ modern

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Vocabulary: comparison से जल्दी याद होती है।

  • ---

    • 5. Nuance Difference System

    (सूक्ष्म अर्थ अंतर प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Important Concept

    दो words similar हो सकते हैं, लेकिन feeling/context अलग हो सकता है।

  • ---

    • Example

    angry

    annoyed

    upset

    furious

  • ---

    • Difference

    annoyed

    → हल्की चिढ़

    angry

    → सामान्य गुस्सा

    furious

    → बहुत ज्यादा गुस्सा

  • ---

    • Example

    look

    see

    watch

  • ---

    • see

    अपने आप दिखाई देना

  • ---

    • look

    जानबूझकर देखना

  • ---

    • watch

    लगातार ध्यान से देखना

  • ---

    • Example

    hear

    listen

  • ---

    • hear

    automatic hearing

  • ---

    • listen

    attention-based hearing

  • ---

    • 6. Emotional Vocabulary System

    (भावनात्मक शब्दावली प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Fear Vocabulary

    afraid

    scared

    terrified

    frightened

    nervous

  • ---

    • Happiness Vocabulary

    happy

    glad

    excited

    delighted

    ecstatic

  • ---

    • Sadness Vocabulary

    sad

    upset

    depressed

    heartbroken

  • ---

    • Confidence Vocabulary

    confident

    bold

    fearless

    self-assured

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Emotion vocabulary: spoken English को powerful बनाती है।

  • ---

    • 7. Formal vs Informal Vocabulary

    (औपचारिक एवं अनौपचारिक शब्दावली)

  • ---

    • InformalFormal

    askinquire

    buypurchase

    helpassist

    startcommence

    endterminate

  • ---

    • Example

    Informal: Can you help me?

    Formal: Could you assist me?

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    हर जगह same vocabulary use नहीं होती।

  • ---

    • 8. Collocation System

    (प्राकृतिक शब्द संयोजन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is Collocation?

    ऐसे words जो naturally साथ उपयोग होते हैं।

  • ---

    • Example

    make a mistake ✅

    do a mistake ❌

  • ---

    • Example

    take a decision ✅

    eat a decision ❌

  • ---

    • Example

    heavy rain ✅

    strong rain ❌

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Vocabulary केवल meaning नहीं है, natural pairing भी है।

  • ---

    • More Collocations

    catch a bus

    break a promise

    make money

    pay attention

    do homework

    take tea

    have tea

    drink water

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    यहीं से: natural English बनती है।

  • ---

    • 9. Powerful Daily Vocabulary System

    (दैनिक शक्तिशाली शब्दावली प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Daily Life Words

    improve

    develop

    achieve

    focus

    discipline

    confidence

    communication

    knowledge

    experience

    opportunity

  • ---

    • Daily Usage

    I want to improve my English.

    Discipline is important for success.

    Practice develops confidence.

  • ---

    • Academic Vocabulary

    analyze

    evaluate

    compare

    explain

    demonstrate

    conclude

  • ---

    • Professional Vocabulary

    meeting

    project

    deadline

    presentation

    strategy

    management

  • ---

    • 10. Vocabulary Usage Drill System

    (शब्दावली प्रयोग अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Word Rotation

    happy

    → glad

    → cheerful

    → delighted

  • ---

    • Sentence Rotation

    I am happy.

    I am glad to meet you.

    She looks cheerful today.

    He was delighted by the result.

  • ---

    • Context Drill

  • ---

    • Angry Situation

    He is angry.

    He is furious.

    He completely lost his temper.

  • ---

    • Sad Situation

    I feel sad.

    I feel upset.

    I am heartbroken.

  • ---

    • Vocabulary Expansion Drill

    small

    → tiny

    → little

    → miniature

    good

    → great

    → excellent

    → outstanding

    bad

    → awful

    → terrible

    → horrible

  • ---

    Vocabulary

    +

    Context

    +

    Nuance

    +

    Collocation

    Emotion

    Part 34 — Idiom, Phrase & Expression System

    (मुहावरा, वाक्यांश एवं अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

    Teacher Introduction

    बच्चों, अब तक हमने:

    grammar

    tense

    spoken English

    translation intelligence

    vocabulary intelligence

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम English के उस भाग में प्रवेश करेंगे जहाँ: language “book English” से निकलकर “real native expression” बनती है।

    क्योंकि: native speakers: हर समय direct sentence नहीं बोलते।

    वे:

    idioms

    phrasal verbs

    expressions

    conversational phrases

    का उपयोग करते हैं।

  • ---

    • 1. Idiom System

    (मुहावरा प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is an Idiom?

    English Definition

    An idiom is a group of words whose meaning is different from the literal meaning of the individual words.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    ऐसा वाक्यांश जिसका अर्थ उसके शब्दों के सीधे अर्थ से अलग हो, उसे idiom कहते हैं।

  • ---

    • Example 1

    Break the ice

  • ---

    • Literal Meaning

    बर्फ तोड़ना

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    बातचीत शुरू करना

    झिझक खत्म करना

  • ---

    • Sentence

    He told a joke to break the ice.

    उसने झिझक खत्म करने के लिए मजाक किया।

  • ---

    • Example 2

    Hit the nail on the head

  • ---

    • Literal Meaning

    कील के सिर पर मारना

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    बिल्कुल सही बात कहना

  • ---

    • Example

    You hit the nail on the head.

    तुमने बिल्कुल सही बात कही।

  • ---

    • Example 3

    Once in a blue moon

  • ---

    • Literal Meaning

    नीले चाँद में एक बार

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    बहुत कम

  • ---

    • Sentence

    He visits us once in a blue moon.

    वह हमसे बहुत कम मिलने आता है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Idioms: direct translation से नहीं समझे जाते।

  • ---

    • 2. Phrasal Verb System

    (वाक्यांश क्रिया प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is a Phrasal Verb?

    Verb + preposition/adverb मिलकर नया meaning बनाते हैं।

  • ---

    • Example 1

    Give up

  • ---

    • Literal Meaning

    दे देना ऊपर

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    हार मान लेना

  • ---

    • Sentence

    Never give up.

    कभी हार मत मानो।

  • ---

    • Example 2

    Look after

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    देखभाल करना

  • ---

    • Sentence

    She looks after her grandmother.

    वह अपनी दादी की देखभाल करती है।

  • ---

    • Example 3

    Run away

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    भाग जाना

  • ---

    • Sentence

    The thief ran away.

    चोर भाग गया।

  • ---

    • Example 4

    Find out

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    पता लगाना

  • ---

    • Sentence

    I found out the truth.

    मुझे सच्चाई पता चल गई।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Phrasal verbs: spoken English में बहुत common हैं।

  • ---

    • 3. Conversational Expression System

    (वार्तालाप अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Greetings

    What’s up?

    क्या हाल है?

    How’s it going?

    सब कैसा चल रहा है?

  • ---

    • Casual Replies

    Not much.

    कुछ खास नहीं।

    Pretty good.

    काफी अच्छा।

  • ---

    • Agreement

    Absolutely!

    बिल्कुल!

    Exactly!

    सही कहा!

  • ---

    • Surprise

    No way!

    ऐसा नहीं हो सकता!

    Seriously?

    सच में?

  • ---

    • Excitement

    Awesome!

    शानदार!

    That’s amazing!

    यह अद्भुत है!

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Conversation English: grammar से ज्यादा expression-driven होती है।

  • ---

    • 4. Daily Spoken Phrase System

    (दैनिक बोलचाल वाक्यांश प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Examples

    Take care.

    अपना ध्यान रखना।

    See you soon.

    जल्दी मिलते हैं।

    Come on!

    चलो!

    Hold on.

    रुको।

    Wait a minute.

    एक मिनट रुको।

    No problem.

    कोई समस्या नहीं।

    Sounds good.

    अच्छा लग रहा है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    ये phrases: daily spoken English की backbone हैं।

  • ---

    • 5. Figurative English System

    (लाक्षणिक अंग्रेज़ी प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    Time is money.

  • ---

    • Literal Meaning

    समय पैसा है।

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    समय बहुत मूल्यवान है।

  • ---

    • Example 2

    He has a heart of stone.

  • ---

    • Literal Meaning

    उसका दिल पत्थर का है।

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    वह बहुत कठोर व्यक्ति है।

  • ---

    • Example 3

    The classroom was a zoo.

  • ---

    • Real Meaning

    कक्षा बहुत शोरगुल वाली थी।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Figurative English: imagination और comparison का उपयोग करती है।

  • ---

    • 6. Emotion-Based Expression System

    (भाव आधारित अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Anger

    I’m fed up with this.

    मैं इससे तंग आ चुका हूँ।

  • ---

    • Happiness

    I’m on cloud nine.

    मैं बहुत खुश हूँ।

  • ---

    • Sadness

    I feel broken.

    मैं अंदर से टूटा हुआ महसूस कर रहा हूँ।

  • ---

    • Fear

    My heart skipped a beat.

    मैं अचानक डर गया।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Emotion expressions: spoken English को natural बनाते हैं।

  • ---

    • 7. Native Reaction Expression System

    (मूल वक्ता प्रतिक्रिया अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Shock

    Oh my God!

    हे भगवान!

  • ---

    • Doubt

    Are you sure?

    क्या तुम्हें यकीन है?

  • ---

    • Disbelief

    You must be kidding.

    तुम मजाक कर रहे हो।

  • ---

    • Appreciation

    That’s impressive.

    यह प्रभावशाली है।

  • ---

    • Sympathy

    That’s unfortunate.

    यह दुर्भाग्यपूर्ण है।

  • ---

    • 8. Formal & Informal Expression System

    (औपचारिक एवं अनौपचारिक अभिव्यक्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • InformalFormal

    ThanksThank you

    ByeGoodbye

    What’s up?How are you?

    SorryI apologize

    Help meCould you assist me?

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    हर situation: same expression नहीं मांगती।

  • ---

    • 9. Contextual Phrase System

    (संदर्भ आधारित वाक्यांश प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • At Restaurant

    Could I see the menu?

    क्या मैं menu देख सकता हूँ?

  • ---

    • At School

    May I come in?

    क्या मैं अंदर आ सकता हूँ?

  • ---

    • On Phone

    Can you hear me clearly?

    क्या आप मुझे साफ सुन पा रहे हैं?

  • ---

    • During Discussion

    I agree with your point.

    मैं आपकी बात से सहमत हूँ।

  • ---

    • During Debate

    I respectfully disagree.

    मैं सम्मानपूर्वक असहमत हूँ।

  • ---

    • 10. Real-Life Expression Drill System

    (वास्तविक जीवन अभिव्यक्ति अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Situation 1 — Excitement

    A: I passed the exam.

    B: That’s amazing!

  • ---

    • Situation 2 — Sympathy

    A: I lost my wallet.

    B: That’s unfortunate.

  • ---

    • Situation 3 — Suggestion

    A: I’m tired.

    B: You should take some rest.

  • ---

    • Situation 4 — Disbelief

    A: I won a lottery.

    B: No way!

  • ---

    • Situation 5 — Encouragement

    A: I’m afraid of speaking English.

    B: Don’t worry. Keep practicing.

  • ---

    • 1. Spotting Error System

    (त्रुटि पहचान प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is Spotting Error?

    Sentence में grammar mistake पहचानना।

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ He do not play cricket.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ He does not play cricket.

  • ---

    • Error Logic

    He/she/it

    → does

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ She are reading a book.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ She is reading a book.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ I have seen him yesterday.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ I saw him yesterday.

  • ---

    • Why Wrong?

    yesterday

    → simple past चाहिए।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive exam: grammar logic test करता है।

  • ---

    • 2. Sentence Improvement System

    (वाक्य सुधार प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example

    ❌ He is more smarter than Ram.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ He is smarter than Ram.

  • ---

    • Why Wrong?

    more + smarter

    दो comparative साथ नहीं आते।

  • ---

    • Example

    ❌ This is the most fastest car.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ This is the fastest car.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    competitive English: small mistakes पकड़ती है।

  • ---

    • 3. Fill in the Blanks System

    (रिक्त स्थान पूर्ति प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    He ___ to school daily.

    (a) go

    (b) goes

    (c) going

    (d) gone

  • ---

    • Correct Answer

    ✅ goes

  • ---

    • Why?

    He/she/it + V5/s/es

  • ---

    • Example 2

    I ___ English now.

    (a) study

    (b) studied

    (c) am studying

    (d) studies

  • ---

    • Correct Answer

    ✅ am studying

  • ---

    • Why?

    now

    → present continuous

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Keywords: tense पहचानने में मदद करते हैं।

  • ---

    • 4. Cloze Test System

    (गद्य रिक्त स्थान प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is Cloze Test?

    एक paragraph में blanks भरना।

  • ---

    • Example

    Ram ___ to school daily.

    He ___ very honest.

  • ---

    • Answers

    goes

    is

  • ---

    • Skills Needed

    grammar

    vocabulary

    context understanding

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Cloze test: grammar + meaning दोनों test करता है।

  • ---

    • 5. Para Jumble System

    (वाक्य क्रम प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is Para Jumble?

    उल्टे sentences को सही क्रम में लगाना।

  • ---

    • Example

    (A) He went to the market.

    (B) Then he bought some fruits.

    (C) Ram woke up early.

  • ---

    • Correct Order

    C → A → B

  • ---

    • Logic

    पहले उठेगा, फिर बाजार जाएगा, फिर फल खरीदेगा।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Sequence understanding: बहुत जरूरी है।

  • ---

    • 6. Phrase Replacement System

    (वाक्यांश प्रतिस्थापन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example

    ❌ He discussed about the problem.

  • ---

    • Correct Replacement

    ✅ He discussed the problem.

  • ---

    • Example

    ❌ Return back soon.

  • ---

    • Correct Replacement

    ✅ Return soon.

  • ---

    • Example

    ❌ Revert back to me.

  • ---

    • Correct Replacement

    ✅ Reply to me.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive English: awkward Indian English पकड़ती है।

  • ---

    • 7. Grammar Trap System

    (व्याकरण जाल प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ One of the boys are absent.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ One of the boys is absent.

  • ---

    • Why?

    Main subject: one

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ Neither Ram nor his friends was present.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ Neither Ram nor his friends were present.

  • ---

    • Why?

    nearer subject rule

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ Mathematics are difficult.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ Mathematics is difficult.

  • ---

    • Why?

    subject singular माना जाता है।

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive exams: trap-based grammar पूछते हैं।

  • ---

    • 8. Competitive Tense System

    (प्रतियोगी काल प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ When I reached the station, the train already left.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ When I reached the station, the train had already left.

  • ---

    • Why?

    पहले completed action

    → past perfect

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ I am knowing him.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ I know him.

  • ---

    • Why?

    know

    → stative verb

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ If he will come, I will help him.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ If he comes, I will help him.

  • ---

    • Why?

    conditional sentence rule

  • ---

    • 9. Competitive Article & Preposition System

    (प्रतियोगी आर्टिकल एवं प्रीपोजीशन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Article Example

    ❌ He is best player.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ He is the best player.

  • ---

    • Preposition Example

    ❌ She is married with him.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ She is married to him.

  • ---

    • Example

    ❌ He depends in his parents.

  • ---

    • Correct Sentence

    ✅ He depends on his parents.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Preposition: competitive English का dangerous area है।

  • ---

    • 10. Competitive Drill System

    (प्रतियोगी अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Correct the Sentence

    ❌ She do not know me.

    ✅ She does not know me.

  • ---

    • ❌ I have completed my work yesterday.

    ✅ I completed my work yesterday.

  • ---

    • ❌ He is senior than me.

    ✅ He is senior to me.

  • ---

    • ❌ One of my friend is absent.

    ✅ One of my friends is absent.

  • ---

    • ❌ The sceneries of Kashmir are beautiful.

    ✅ The scenery of Kashmir is beautiful.

  • ---

    • 1. One Word Substitution System

    (एक शब्द प्रतिस्थापन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is One Word Substitution?

    पूरे phrase/sentence को एक word में व्यक्त करना।

  • ---

    • Example 1

    A person who cannot read or write

    ✅ Illiterate

  • ---

    • Example 2

    A person who loves mankind

    ✅ Philanthropist

  • ---

    • Example 3

    A person who knows many languages

    ✅ Linguist

  • ---

    • Example 4

    A government ruled by the people

    ✅ Democracy

  • ---

    • Example 5

    A place where books are kept

    ✅ Library

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive exams: short precise vocabulary पूछते हैं।

  • ---

    • 2. Synonym System

    (समानार्थी शब्द प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    Brave

  • ---

    • Synonyms

    courageous

    fearless

    bold

    valiant

  • ---

    • Example 2

    Happy

  • ---

    • Synonyms

    glad

    cheerful

    delighted

    joyful

  • ---

    • Example 3

    Important

  • ---

    • Synonyms

    significant

    essential

    crucial

    vital

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    हर synonym: हर जगह interchangeable नहीं होता।

  • ---

    • Example

    big mistake ✅

    large mistake ⚠️ awkward

  • ---

    • 3. Antonym System

    (विलोम शब्द प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Examples

    ancient ↔ modern

    victory ↔ defeat

    expand ↔ contract

    accept ↔ reject

    optimistic ↔ pessimistic

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Opposition-based learning: vocabulary जल्दी याद करवाती है।

  • ---

    • 4. Idiom & Phrase Competitive System

    (प्रतियोगी मुहावरा एवं वाक्यांश प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    At the eleventh hour

  • ---

    • Meaning

    अंतिम समय पर

  • ---

    • Sentence

    He completed the work at the eleventh hour.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    A blessing in disguise

  • ---

    • Meaning

    छिपा हुआ लाभ

  • ---

    • Example 3

    Burn the midnight oil

  • ---

    • Meaning

    देर रात तक पढ़ना/काम करना

  • ---

    • Example 4

    Call a spade a spade

  • ---

    • Meaning

    सीधी बात कहना

  • ---

    • Example 5

    Hit the nail on the head

  • ---

    • Meaning

    बिल्कुल सही बात कहना

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive exams: idiomatic meaning पूछते हैं, literal meaning नहीं।

  • ---

    • 5. Confusing Word System

    (भ्रमित करने वाले शब्द प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    Affect vs Effect

  • ---

    • Affect

    verb

    प्रभाव डालना

  • ---

    • Example

    The weather affected my health.

  • ---

    • Effect

    noun

    प्रभाव/परिणाम

  • ---

    • Example

    The effect was terrible.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    Advice vs Advise

  • ---

    • Advice

    noun

    सलाह

  • ---

    • Advise

    verb

    सलाह देना

  • ---

    • Example 3

    Principal vs Principle

  • ---

    • Principal

    मुख्य व्यक्ति

    विद्यालय प्रधानाचार्य

  • ---

    • Principle

    सिद्धांत

  • ---

    • Example 4

    Accept vs Except

  • ---

    • Accept

    स्वीकार करना

  • ---

    • Except

    को छोड़कर

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive English: similar-looking words से trap बनाती है।

  • ---

    • 6. Spelling Intelligence System

    (वर्तनी बुद्धिमत्ता प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Common Competitive Spellings

    separate

    necessary

    government

    environment

    opportunity

    recommend

    embarrass

    pronunciation

  • ---

    • Common Wrong Spellings

    ❌ goverment

    ✅ government

  • ---

    • ❌ seperate

    ✅ separate

  • ---

    • ❌ enviroment

    ✅ environment

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Spelling: pattern recognition से मजबूत होती है।

  • ---

    • 7. Vocabulary Trap System

    (शब्दावली जाल प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example 1

    ❌ He is my cousin brother.

  • ---

    • Correct

    ✅ He is my cousin.

  • ---

    • Example 2

    ❌ Discuss about this issue.

  • ---

    • Correct

    ✅ Discuss this issue.

  • ---

    • Example 3

    ❌ Return back.

  • ---

    • Correct

    ✅ Return.

  • ---

    • Example 4

    ❌ Repeat again.

  • ---

    • Correct

    ✅ Repeat.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Competitive English: redundancy errors पकड़ती है।

  • ---

    • 8. Context-Based Vocabulary System

    (संदर्भ आधारित शब्दावली प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Word

    Bright

  • ---

    • Different Meanings by Context

  • ---

    • Intelligent

    He is a bright student.

  • ---

    • Shining

    The room was bright.

  • ---

    • Hopeful

    The future looks bright.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Vocabulary: context बदलने से meaning बदल सकता है।

  • ---

    • Another Example

    Light

  • ---

    • कम वजन

    This bag is light.

  • ---

    • प्रकाश

    The light is on.

  • ---

    • हल्का रंग

    She likes light colors.

  • ---

    • 9. High Frequency Competitive Vocabulary

    (उच्च आवृत्ति प्रतियोगी शब्दावली)

    achieve

  • ---

    • 10. Final Competitive Vocabulary Drill System

    (अंतिम प्रतियोगी शब्दावली अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Choose the Correct Word

    He gave me good ______.

    (a) advise

    (b) advice

    ✅ advice

  • ---

    • Choose the Correct Meaning

    “At the eleventh hour” means:

    (a) early

    (b) at the last moment

    (c) happily

    (d) angrily

    ✅ at the last moment

  • ---

    • Correct the Sentence

    ❌ He discussed about politics.

    ✅ He discussed politics.

  • ---

    • ❌ She returned back yesterday.

    ✅ She returned yesterday.

  • ---

    • One Word Substitution

    A person who cannot see

    ✅ blind

  • ---

    • Synonym

    Huge

    ✅ enormous

  • ---

    • Antonym

    Victory

    ✅ defeat

  • ---

    • Final Competitive Vocabulary Formula

    Vocabulary

    +

    Context

    +

    Usage

    +

    Precision

    +

    Pattern Recognition

    +

    Exam Awareness

    Competitive Vocabulary Mastery

    Student:

    competitive vocabulary मजबूत कर सके

    vocabulary traps पकड़ सके

    exam-oriented English mastery विकसित कर सके।

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम English के उस भाग में प्रवेश करेंगे जहाँ: language “answer देने” से आगे बढ़कर:

    writing

    presentation

    communication

    expression

    creativity

    का माध्यम बनती है।

    Student:

    proper English writing कर सके

    1. Paragraph Writing System

  • ---

    • 1. Paragraph Writing System

    (अनुच्छेद लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is a Paragraph?

    English Definition

    A paragraph is a group of sentences that develops one main idea.

  • ---

    • Hindi Definition

    ऐसे वाक्यों का समूह जो एक मुख्य विचार को विकसित करे, paragraph कहलाता है।

  • ---

    • Structure of Paragraph

    1. Topic Sentence

    2. Supporting Sentences

    3. Concluding Sentence

  • ---

    • Example Topic

    Importance of Discipline

  • ---

    • Paragraph

    Discipline is very important in life. It helps a person stay focused and organized. A disciplined student studies regularly and respects time. Discipline also develops confidence and responsibility. Without discipline, success becomes difficult. Therefore, discipline is the key to success.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Good paragraph:

    one idea

    clear flow

    proper ending

    रखता है।

  • ---

    • 2. Essay Writing System

    (निबंध लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Essay Structure

    1. Introduction

    2. Body

    3. Conclusion

  • ---

    • Example Topic

    Importance of English

  • ---

    • Introduction

    English is one of the most important languages in the world. It is used in education, business, science, and communication.

  • ---

    • Body

    English helps people communicate internationally. It also provides better career opportunities. Most modern knowledge and technology are available in English.

  • ---

    • Conclusion

    Therefore, learning English is essential in the modern world.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Essay: paragraph से बड़ा और detailed होता है।

  • ---

    • 3. Letter Writing System

    (पत्र लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Types of Letters

    1. Formal Letter

    2. Informal Letter

  • ---

    • Formal Letter

    To

    The Principal

    ABC School

    Subject: Leave Application

    Respected Sir,

    I am suffering from fever. Therefore, I request you to grant me leave for two days.

    Thank you.

    Yours obediently,

    Ram

  • ---

    • Informal Letter

    Dear Friend,

    How are you? I hope you are doing well. I miss you very much.

    Your friend,

    Mohan

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Formal और informal tone अलग होती है।

  • ---

    • 4. Email Writing System

    (ईमेल लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Structure

    To

    Subject

    Greeting

    Main Message

    Closing

  • ---

    • Example

    Subject: Meeting Confirmation

    Dear Sir,

    I am writing to confirm tomorrow’s meeting. I will arrive on time.

    Thank you.

    Regards,

    Rahul

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Email: modern formal communication का important part है।

  • ---

    • 5. Notice Writing System

    (सूचना लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • What is Notice?

    Short official information.

  • ---

    • Example

    NOTICE

    All students are informed that the school will remain closed tomorrow due to heavy rain.

    Principal

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Notice:

    short

    clear

    direct

    होता है।

  • ---

    • 6. Report Writing System

    (प्रतिवेदन लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example Topic

    Annual Sports Day

  • ---

    • Report

    Our school celebrated Annual Sports Day on Monday. Many students participated in different games and competitions. The principal encouraged the students to maintain sportsmanship. The program ended successfully.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Report: real event का factual description होता है।

  • ---

    • 7. Article Writing System

    (लेख लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Example Topic

    Importance of Reading Books

  • ---

    • Article

    Reading books improves knowledge and imagination. It develops vocabulary and thinking ability. Books also help us understand different cultures and ideas. Therefore, reading should become a daily habit.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Article: information + opinion दोनों देता है।

  • ---

    • 8. Creative Writing System

    (सृजनात्मक लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Story Writing

    Once upon a time, there was a poor farmer who worked very hard. One day, he found a bag full of gold coins…

  • ---

    • Dialogue Writing

    Ram: Where are you going?

    Mohan: I am going to the market.

  • ---

    • Imaginative Writing

    If I became a scientist, I would invent machines to help poor farmers.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Creative writing: imagination develop करती है।

  • ---

    • 9. Formal vs Informal Writing System

    (औपचारिक एवं अनौपचारिक लेखन प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • InformalFormal

    ThanksThank you

    ByeGoodbye

    Can’tCannot

    Help meKindly assist me

  • ---

    • Example

    Informal: I can’t come today.

    Formal: I am unable to attend today.

  • ---

    • Important Understanding

    Writing style: situation के अनुसार बदलती है।

  • ---

    • 10. Writing Improvement Drill System

    (लेखन सुधार अभ्यास प्रणाली)

  • ---

    • Weak Sentence

    I am very happy.

  • ---

    • Better Sentence

    I am extremely delighted.

  • ---

    • Weak Sentence

    He is a good boy.

  • ---

    • Better Sentence

    He is a disciplined and hardworking student.

  • ---

    • Sentence Expansion Drill

    Basic: The boy runs.

    Expanded: The young boy runs quickly toward the playground every morning.

  • ---

    • Error Correction Drill

    ❌ He go to school daily.

    ✅ He goes to school daily.

  • ---

    • ❌ I am having a car.

    ✅ I have a car.

  • ---

    • Final Writing Formula

    Grammar

    +

    Vocabulary

    +

    Structure

    +

    Clarity

    +

    Creativity

    +

    Natural Expression

    Effective English Writing

  • ---

    • Final Goal of Part 37

    Student:

    paragraph लिख सके

    essay लिख सके

    formal/informal writing समझ सके

    letter/email/report लिख सके

    creative writing कर सके

    structured composition बना सके

    writing mistakes सुधार सके

    expressive English writing mastery विकसित कर सके।

    grammar

    idioms

    writing system

    समझ लिया।

    अब हम English के अंतिम practical स्तर में प्रवेश करेंगे जहाँ: language केवल subject नहीं, बल्कि:

    personality

    communication

    professional life

    public interaction

    leadership

    का माध्यम बनती है।

    1. Self Introduction System

    2. Interview English System

    3. Public Speaking System
